Solar Eclipse to be Seen in the South Pacific 51

This Month on the 21st and 22nd

Scientists Prepare for Observation

The World News reports that there will be a solar eclipse on the 21st and 22nd of this month, which can be seen in the islands of the South Pacific. Part of the solar eclipse begins at sunset on the 21st and ends at sunrise on the 22nd. It can be seen from Cape Horn in South America to Western Australia. However, the total solar eclipse can only be seen on the island of Tin Can, 300 miles north of the Tonga Islands, and on another small island, and it will only last for 92 seconds. For academic research purposes, the US Navy has sent three small ships carrying the observation team organized by the US Weights and Measures Bureau, the Rohs Foundation, and the Carnegie Institution, as well as various applied scientific instruments, to Tin Can Island. At the same time, many scientists in New Zealand and Australia are also preparing for observation. The American observation team consists of 20 people. At that time, the main task will be to photograph the atmosphere around the solar sphere.

Domestic News

Sun Lianzhong Sends Representative to Shandong 52

To Request Han Fuju to Plead Loyalty to the Central Government on His Behalf

Jinan Correspondence: The Central Plains War and the disintegration of the Northwest Army have now reached a stage of political resolution. All Northwest Army personnel who have surrendered have been appointed to various positions, while the majority of Feng's army who retreated to Hebei have been reporting their willingness to surrender and be incorporated into the national army in recent days. Yesterday (the 16th), Li Han-hui, the chief of staff of Sun Lianzhong, an important general of the Northwest Army, arrived in Jinan from Xinxiang on behalf of Sun Lianzhong to report the situation at the front to Han Fuju and Jiang Bocheng and request them to plead loyalty to the Central Government on his behalf. Han and Jiang immediately telegraphed the Central Government to request instructions. In his telegram, Han strongly stated that he had worked with Sun Lianzhong for many years in the Northwest Army and knew him very well. This surrender is sincere and he guaranteed that Sun would never go back on his word. Today, a reply telegram was received from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, ordering Jiang Bocheng to go to Nanjing with Sun's representative for face-to-face consultations to avoid repeated telegram exchanges. After receiving the telegram, Jiang and Han agreed with Li Han-hui and decided to take the Jinpu train to Nanjing tomorrow morning. It is said that Han told Jiang Bocheng that Sun Lianzhong (Sun Lianzhong's given name) is a fellow villager and colleague and knows him to be honest and reliable. He urged Jiang to plead with the Commander-in-Chief for extra understanding. All other issues will be subject to the orders of the Central Government. However, regarding the issue of garrisoning, he can obey orders to go to any place north of the Yangtze River. If he is transferred to the south of the Yangtze River, Sun's basic forces can also obey, but he is afraid that the newly attached forces cannot be commanded as desired. This is Sun's unavoidable predicament. The reporter visited Mr. Li Han-hui today and asked about the recent situation of the Northwest Army. According to Li, Sun's headquarters has a total of four divisions. There was no major loss in this retreat. Sun and his three men are currently stationed in Xinxiang, and the troops are stationed in Xinxiang and along the Daokou-Qinghua Railway. The remaining Northwest Army personnel who retreated to the north of the Yellow River include the units of Liu Chunrong, Sun Liangcheng, Liu Guitang, Sun Dianying, and Zheng Dazhang. Each unit has suffered considerable losses, but Sun Liangcheng's unit has only a pistol brigade left after Ji Hongchang and Liang Kouying defected. Feng Yuxiang, seeing that the general trend was over, left Xinxiang's Nanxiaoji Town on the 9th with four or five followers and went west. Before I came to Jinan, I did not know his whereabouts. Lu Zhonglin has also voluntarily stepped down. Sun Liangcheng has also decided to step down due to the huge losses. All the above-mentioned troops are under the command of Sun Lianzhong. Since Sun's headquarters has no way out and the troops under his command still have more than 20,000 people, he sent me to Jinan to ask Chairman Han to plead with the Central Government for surrender in order to end the responsibility and end the war as soon as possible. As for the units of Song Zheyuan and Liu Yufen, they have retreated to Shaanxi. (October 17)

He Jinbiao and Lu Xingming Captured 53

He Has Been Executed and Lu Will Be Sent to the Province

Fuzhou Correspondence: Liu Zongyi of the First Provincial Police Brigade recaptured Songzheng yesterday. He Jinbiao, the chief bandit of the Lu army who had surrendered, seeing that Lu's troops were collapsing, went from Zhenghe to Yanping to see Lu Xingbang, intending to rush to the Zhejiang border to command his troops and take the road through Zhenghe to collect the remnants. It happened that his former subordinate Ye Songsheng heard about it and brought guards to watch at the location He had to pass through. On the 9th, He and his eight guards were intercepted and reported to Liu Zongyi, who telegraphed the province for instructions. The provincial government telegraphed back ordering him to send He to the province for interrogation. Liu had already escorted He to Sandu on the 11th. However, the provincial government then considered that He had harassed the Fuzhou Ningfu area for a long time and had now been captured alive and should be shot immediately. It specifically telegraphed Jin Zhenzhong, the brigade commander of the Marine Corps stationed in Sandu, to execute He on the spot. Jin obeyed the order and shot He on the 13th and reported it to the province.

After the June 1st coup, Lu and Ming went to Shanghai to show that they had not joined the coup and remained as a last resort for a turnaround. Recently, Lu Xingming, seeing that Lu Xingbang and Lu Xingrong had telegraphed their resignation, went from Shanghai to Zhejiang and returned to Yanping to consult with Lu's generals in order to seek peace through the mediation of Sun Benrong. Lu Xingbang Requests Surrender to the Fujian Provincial Government 54

Liu Heding and the Party Department Advocate Rejection

Fang Shengtao Advocates Both Suppression and Pacification

Fuzhou Correspondence: Lu Xingbang recently sent a telegram to the province requesting surrender due to repeated defeats. The telegram arrived in the province on the 9th, stating that the changes of the 16th were originally a political issue, but unexpectedly the war broke out, and the people upstream and downstream were devastated. I deeply regret it. I have telegraphed my resignation and requested a ceasefire, and sent personnel to Youxi to discuss the receiving method. According to Lu Xingrong, the commander of the Fifth Brigade, this war has caused great suffering to the soldiers and civilians. I have resigned from my post and submitted a joint telegram. After receiving the telegram, Yang Shuzhuang convened the generals Liu Heding, Fang Shengtao, Chen Jiliang, and Yang Tingjing in the provincial government in the afternoon to discuss response measures. Fang Shengtao advocated first sending out the six captured people, and then concentrating the troops in Youxi to await orders. Liu Heding believed that the military procedure had been more than halfway through, and the elimination of Lu's troops was only in the final battle, and there was no reason to compromise halfway. As a result, Yang Shuzhuang telegraphed the National Government for instructions. At the same time, Yan Er'ai, the deputy division commander of Liu's troops, and the brigade commanders Liu Shangzhi, Lin Shouguo, and Qian Yuguang, also stated that after the capture of Shuikou Huangtian, the first phase of the war was over, and they took this opportunity to reorganize their troops and temporarily suspend the attack, and on the 10th and 11th, they came to the province from the front line to discuss the second phase of the attack on Yanping. Fang Shengtao and Sun Benrong took a steamer to Xiamen and then to Yongchun via Quanzhou, and met with Zhang Zhen, the commander of the newly organized First Division, and decided on the military plan for the western front. The provincial party department still advocated thorough suppression. On the 12th, they again sent two members, Zhan Diaoyuan and Wang Huaijin, to visit Yang Shuzhuang and ask him to strictly order the commanders of the eastern and western fronts to thoroughly eradicate Lu's army. Yang replied that he would convene a joint meeting of the party, government, and military at 2:00 p.m. on the 13th to resolve the issue. After this meeting, a concrete decision on Lu's policy can be made. However, it is said that Lu's final plan is that if peace cannot be achieved, he will lead the remnants of his troops to retreat to the border areas where Fujian, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi provinces meet in order to protect himself. He has now contacted Lin Shouchang and He Jinbiao on the Zhejiang border and Wei Chu and Zhou Guanhong on the Jiangxi border. The authorities in Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces should take precautions. (October 13)

Xiamen Correspondence: The downstream troops attacking Lu have temporarily stopped advancing after capturing Dehua. Military Commissioner Fang Shengtao promoted to the province on September 22, and discussed all plans with Yang Shuzhuang, Liu Heding, and Chen Jiliang, and negotiated Lu Xingming's surrender, and requested the payment of salaries and bullets for the downstream troops. He did not return to Xiamen by steamer until the 10th of this month. It is said that the results of Fang's promotion to the province that the outside world knows are: (1) Sun Benrong represented Lu Xingming to the province to negotiate surrender and incorporation, and there are already some clues. The provincial government proposed that Lu Xingbang immediately resign, first release the five provincial commissioners, and Lu's troops listen to reorganization; (2) Request the Central Government to send four regiments of capable troops to enter Fujian from Zhejiang to cooperate in suppressing Lu. If Lu does not comply, it will be resolved by force; (3) The plan to attack Lu has been slightly changed, and it is divided into four routes: (A) Taking the route from Shuikou, with Liu Heding as the commander-in-chief; (B) Taking the route from Dehua to Datian, with Fang Shengtao as the commander-in-chief, the target is first Youxi, then Yanping; (C) Going straight from Gutian, with Chen Jiliang or Chen Wantai as the commander-in-chief; (D) The Central Government sends four regiments of troops to take the route to Pucheng, the target of these two routes is Yanping. Fang returned to Quanzhou from Xiamen on the 11th and went to the front line in Dehua to command the troops to attack Datian. That is, while negotiating surrender and pacification, he still sends troops to implement both suppression and pacification, hoping to end the war as soon as possible. In addition, Fang and Yang Shuzhuang discussed reorganizing the provincial defense army's training regiment into a brigade and assigning it to the newly organized First Division as the Fifth Brigade. It is said that Yang has agreed. (October 13)

Hankou Announces the Lifting of Martial Law 55

Wuchang and Hanyang Continue as Before

Hankou Correspondence: The Wuhan Garrison Command has been under martial law for several months since it was announced. Now the military at the front has come to an end, and the security of Wuhan is becoming more and more consolidated. A special request has been submitted to the Wuhan Headquarters to announce the lifting of martial law. According to the headquarters' instructions, the Hankou area is allowed to relax the night curfew first, while Wuchang and Hanyang will continue as before. After receiving the order, the department issued a notice to all citizens on the 18th, announcing the lifting of martial law in Hankou. The notice is as follows: "Previously, during the military period, we successively obeyed the orders of the headquarters, and Wuhan announced the lifting of martial law, from 12:00 p.m. to 5:00 a.m. the next morning, all traffic was cut off. For several months, thanks to the efforts of the military and police and the assistance of the people, the city has been peaceful and safe. Now that Yan Feng and the other rebels have completely collapsed, the military is about to end, and our troops at the front have been transferred to Hubei in order to suppress bandits and garrison troops. The security of Wuhan is becoming more and more consolidated. This department has considered the situation and submitted a request to the headquarters to open all three districts of Wuhan to traffic from 12:00 p.m. to the next morning, or to relax the night curfew in the Hankou district first, in order to facilitate the departure of merchants and civilians. Now, we have received an order that martial law in the Wuchang and Hanyang districts should continue as before, and that the Hankou district should be allowed to relax the night curfew first, but still needs to be secretly guarded, etc. In addition to the fact that the Wuchang and Hanyang districts are still under martial law and will remain as before, the Hankou district should relax the night curfew from today, in addition to ordering subordinates to comply, this notice is hereby issued for public knowledge. (October 18)

Explosion at the Japanese Concession Power Plant 56

The Municipal Government Has Lodged a Protest with the Japanese Consulate

Hankou Dispatch, October 3, 6 PM: A boiler exploded at the power plant of the Japanese Residents' Group in the Japanese Concession of Hankou, resulting in casualties among Chinese people and considerable property damage. The Municipal Government ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate. The investigation revealed that four people, including Wang Xinghe, died, more than ten were seriously injured, and other property damage was extensive. Yesterday, the Municipal Government sent a letter to the Japanese Consul-General in Hankou, requesting that he order separate compensations and condolences to be paid to respect human life. The original letter reads as follows: "Sir, this government received a report from merchants Zhu Xiangtai and Wang Shunchang of Gugu Che, stating that the merchant's two-year-old son, Xinhe, was sitting quietly in the shop around 6 PM on the 3rd of this month when the machine boiler in the Japanese electric lighting room suddenly exploded. He was instantly killed. The police of the 13th Precinct were immediately notified for investigation. The Hankou District Court prosecutor and the Japanese side came to examine the body and confirmed that he died from the explosion. An injury report was filed. The merchant is over thirty years old and this was his only son. It is truly unbearable that he was tragically killed in the explosion. It is appropriate to request a prompt and serious negotiation to respect human life, etc. This government ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate and respond for review and issued a notification. Subsequently, the Public Security Bureau reported that the Japanese Residents' Group's power plant boiler explosion resulted in the death and injury of many Chinese people and requested a review. Considering that the reported details were not clear, this government further ordered the relevant police precinct to promptly and thoroughly investigate and report the cause of the incident, the treatment of the injured, and the losses of nearby merchants. Now, the Bureau has responded, stating that the relevant police precinct was ordered to investigate and report within two days after receiving the order. Now, the Precinct Chief, Wan Dixiu, has reported that he immediately dispatched Inspector Xia Duokui to investigate and clarify the situation. He reported that the location of the incident was within the concession and the Chinese people generally claimed ignorance. However, relatives of the power plant workers said that at 6:15 PM on the 3rd of this month, the Japanese Residents' Group's power plant boiler exploded. It was confirmed that Boiler No. 3 was rusty. Additionally, the fire was excessive that night, and the steam pressure became too high, causing the boiler to explode, collapsing the surrounding houses. Therefore, flying bricks and stones injured pedestrians and damaged nearby houses. An investigation was conducted at the affected houses and the power plant, resulting in substantial findings of injuries to people and property damage. In addition to submitting a list of damaged property and diagnosis reports for the injured, all information regarding the Japanese Concession Residents' Group's power plant boiler explosion, injuries to Chinese people, and property damage is respectfully reported for review. Attached are lists of damaged property and a list of injured names from the Japanese Concession Red Cross Hospital. Following prior orders, the original lists are copied and respectfully submitted for your review. The attached tables are submitted for review and referral for negotiation." Attached are two copies of the tables. "Based on this, it is found that the Residents' Group's power plant boiler explosion resulted in deaths, injuries, and property damage. The responsible personnel failed to take preventative measures and neglected their duties. If no order is given for separate compensations and condolences to be paid, human life will not be respected, and there will be no warning. Based on the reported information, in addition to informing the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and issuing instructions, copies of the original tables are enclosed and respectfully requested to be reviewed and handled. (October 17)"

Preliminary Judicial Examination Held in Guangdong 57

Examination Scheduled for the 24th at the High Court

Guangzhou Dispatch: Recently, the National Government promulgated the Provisional Regulations for Preliminary Judicial Examinations and appointed Zhu Lǚhe as the Chief Examiner, and Xie Yingzhou, Luo Wenzhuang, and Huang Jilu as Examination Committee Members. The Preliminary Judicial Examination Committee has also recently established a branch in Guangzhou, appointing Huang Jilu, the Provincial Propaganda Minister, and Luo Wenzhuang, the President of the High Court, as Examination Committee Members. Lawyers Cao Shoukun and Du Zhizhi, and law professor Xue Sixian, etc., were hired as Assistant Examiners. The screening examination is scheduled for the 24th of this month at the High Court. This judicial examination is the second. The first one was held in Guangzhou in 1926. All those who passed have been assigned to positions such as clerks in courts at all levels. Subsequently, the Ministry of Judicial Administration established a judicial training institute in the capital, which continued to enroll students from Guangdong. The first class of graduates, including Liu Yanping and others, have been assigned to serve in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Guangdong provinces. The location, date, registration, and eligibility requirements for this Guangzhou screening examination have been announced by the High Court. The appendix is as follows. For announcement, the Jia telegram from the Preliminary Judicial Examination Committee of the Judicial Officer states: "The admission test for students of the Judicial Training Institute has been changed to the Preliminary Judicial Examination. The National Government has promulgated the Judicial Officer Preliminary Examination Regulations and specially appointed Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Judicial Administration as the Chief Examiner, and briefly appointed Vice-Minister Xie and President Luo of your court (President Luo Wenzhuang of the Guangdong High Court), Mr. Huang Jilu, etc. as Examiners. The Examination Committee was established in the Ministry of Judicial Administration on Geng Day of this month. Hope to establish a Guangdong branch of the Preliminary Judicial Examination Committee of Judicial Officers, issue and use the official seal, and report to Beijing. The screening test is scheduled to begin on Hao Day of this month. The Guangzhou examination is scheduled to begin on Jing (24th) day of this month. Registration is still allowed three days before the screening test. The screening test will be drafted by the branch, and the examination will be drafted by this committee. Specialist sent. In addition to the Provisional Regulations for the Judicial Officer Examination and Examination Regulations, etc., will be copied and sent separately, and staff will be sent immediately to carry the test papers. This is a special telegram." Based on this, in addition to following the telegram to establish the Guangdong Branch of the Preliminary Judicial Examination Committee of Judicial Officers to handle all matters related to enrollment and examination, and in addition to waiting for the promulgation and issuance of the Provisional Regulations for the Judicial Officer Examination and Examination Regulations, registration will begin on the 16th of this month. All persons who meet the eligibility requirements and are interested in taking the examination should bring their commission certificates and other documents to the court for registration within the deadline to await the examination. Do not delay. Announcing here, detailed information: (1) Eligibility requirements: Graduates with certificates from national or registered public universities, independent colleges, or vocational schools, and foreign universities, independent colleges, or vocational schools recognized by the Ministry of Education who have studied law and political science for more than three years, or who have taught civil and criminal law, national government organizational law, administrative law, commercial law regulations, international public law, etc. at such schools for more than two years, or who have studied law and political science at such schools for more than one year, obtained a graduation certificate, and have served in judicial affairs for more than two years, or court recording affairs for more than three years, are eligible to register for the examination. (2) Registration Location: Guangdong Branch of the Preliminary Judicial Examination Committee of Judicial Officers. (3) Registration Date: From October 16, 1929, to three days before the test (i.e., October 21). (4) Registration Procedures: Submit four recent four-inch half-length photos of oneself, and school diploma, employment letter, appointment letter, party membership certificate (those who have not joined the party should fill out a party membership application), etc. (October 12)

Liu Jianxu Supervises the Suppression of Communist Bandits in Changsha-Yueyang 58

Changsha Dispatch: After the Communist bandits Peng Dehuai, Huang Gonglue, Zhu De, and Mao Zedong and their gangs fled into Jiangxi, the gangs of Kong Hechong and Li Baoxing continued to occupy the two counties of Pingjiang and Liuyang, and spread to various towns and villages in Yueyang, Xiangyin, and Changsha, wantonly disturbing the people. The counties have requested the authorities to take advantage of the fact that the large Communist bandit gangs have fled into Jiangxi to quickly dispatch troops to suppress the Communist bandits in Changsha, Yueyang, Pingjiang, and Liuyang to prevent them from spreading. Before He Yingqin went from Hankou to Zhengzhou, he also telegraphed He Jian, urging him to quickly suppress the Communist bandits. Yesterday, He Jian convened a military conference at the General Headquarters, deciding to assign the Independent 7th Brigade of Chen Guangzhong and the Liuyang Security Team to suppress the Communist bandits in Liuyang, and the 31st Division of Tao Guang, the 15th Division of Hou Pengfei, the Independent Regiment of the Headquarters of Ye Wenke, the First Suppression Battalion of Guo Bugao, the Third Suppression Battalion of Zhu Xingshu, and the Training Regiment of the 16th Division of Li Bingguo to suppress the Communist bandits along the railway line and in the three counties of Xiangyin, Yueyang, and Pingjiang. All the above units were mobilized simultaneously on the 15th to carry out the suppression within a month. All the current suppression units, and the local defense volunteer teams in the five counties of Changsha, Yueyang, Pingjiang, Liuyang, and Xiangyin, are under the command of Liu Jianxu, the commander of the 28th Army, who is responsible for overall planning and suppression, in order to unify authority. The units have departed one after another. Chen Guangzhong is marching towards Liuyang. The 31st Division of Tao Guang has concentrated in Yuezhou. The 15th Division of Hou Pengfei has concentrated in Miluo. The troops have defeated the gang of Kong Hechong, who destroyed the railway. All of the area from Miluo, Taolin, Huangsha Street, Rongjiawan, and Matang to Yuezhou has been cleared. The Hunan-Hubei train can pass today (17th). It is reported that the Communist bandits have fled to Changle, on the border between Pingjiang and Xiangyin. Tao Guang, Hou Pengfei, and Zhong Guangren have arrived in Miluo to discuss suppression measures. Since the Communist bandits in Hunan are only the two major gangs of Kong (Hechong) and Li (Baoxing), both concentrated in the Pingjiang area, the subsequent suppression is extremely important. Liu Jianxu took the Xiang-E armored train from Changsha to Miluo at 12:00 AM on the 16th to supervise and direct the suppression, and instructed Tao Guang and Hou Pengfei on the suppression strategy. In total, there are around 20 regiments of suppression troops, so they should be able to complete the suppression on schedule. (October 17)

Lu Dipin Has Gone to Beijing for Instructions

Communist Bandits in Yuanhe and Ganjiang Totally Retreat

On the 11th, 12th, and 13th, the Zhu-Mao bandit army attacked Zhangshu, with great ferocity. On the government side, the defense line started from Niuxing Station, passed through Gao'an Qingjiangkou, and crossed the Ganjiang River to Xingan. There were fierce battles for several days. In addition to firing intense artillery, the government army had two aircraft that dropped bombs to help in the battle. Therefore, the defense in eastern Jiangxi is strained. The New 13th Division arrived in Fuzhou on the 16th. Division Commander Deng rushed to Fuzhou from the province on the 17th to direct. Regarding the bandit suppression troops coming to Jiangxi, the 148th Brigade of the 50th Division of Cheng Guangyao arrived in Xun yesterday. The 150th Brigade of Luo Shouyi has all arrived in the province. The division headquarters and direct subordinate units are stationed in the provincial capital, successively heading to the front to suppress the bandits. The 60th Brigade of Li Hualing of the Xu Kexiang Division, the 115th and 119th Regiments, arrived in Xun yesterday and will arrive in the province tomorrow. The Luo Lin and Li Jue units of the Hunan Army chasing the bandits have already passed Yuanzhou and are advancing rapidly towards Fenyi. The two divisions of Tao Guang and Qian Dajun are also being transported from Hankou to Xun and then to the province. The Jin Handing, Mao Bingwen, and Li Yunjie divisions are also preparing to come to Jiangxi in sequence. In total, there are more than ten divisions of the above units, and all the Communist bandits can be uprooted, eliminating future troubles forever. (October 17)

Resolution of Boundary Demarcation Issue Between Jinan City and Counties 60

Jinan Dispatch: The boundary demarcation issue between Jinan City and Licheng County has been in dispute for many days and has not been resolved. A boundary demarcation committee was specially organized to re-demarcate the boundary. The committee began demarcation on the 7th of this month. The participants included Li Weixia, representative of the Department of Civil Affairs; Hu Jingxi, representative of the Department of Construction; Mei Baokui, representative of the County Government; Li Quanben, representative of the Municipal Government; Wu Chunyuan and Zhao Jinming, representatives of the Bureau of Finance; Huang Kui, representative of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Ye Qi, representative of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works; and four surveyors and eleven mounted police officers. They first went to Renjia Shankou, taking the Changqing boundary marker as Jinan City Boundary Marker No. 1. Next, they went to Da Yangjia Village, taking the Zhu Jiazhuang stone tablet east of the village as Jinan City Boundary Marker No. 2. Then they went to Da Yinma Village, taking the Chen Hanyuan family's well stone west of the village as Jinan City Boundary Marker No. 3. They returned to the Municipal Government that day. They set off at 8:00 AM on the 8th, first going to Xisha Wang Village. The east and west of this village belong to Changqing, and the middle belongs to Licheng. For administrative convenience, the entire village was assigned to Jinan City, taking the stone next to the well west of the village as City Boundary Marker No. 4. Next, they went to Da Lujia Village, taking the large tree along the Yellow River northwest of the village as City Boundary Marker No. 5, with the center of the Yellow River as the northern boundary. At 9:00 AM on the morning of the 11th, the participants gathered at the Third Branch Bureau of Public Security in Dongweizi Men and set off, first going to Xiaojiezi along the Yellow River, taking the large Yang tree in Anjia Village in the northeast corner as City Boundary Marker No. 6. Next, they went to the stone bridge next to the Houfeng Well on the Xiaoxiaoqing River bank east of Fanjia Garden, taking it as City Boundary Marker No. 7. Going south to Da Xin Village, they took the stone bridge next to the Xu Liuzhu Well east of the village as City Boundary Marker No. 8. Returning west to Bajian Fort, they took the stone bridge next to the Fan Changhe Well east of the village as City Boundary Marker No. 9. They returned to the city at 5:00 PM. On the 13th, they gathered at Dongweizi Men again and set off eastward to Xianfu Village, taking the corner of the stone wall east of the village as City Boundary Marker No. 10. Going south to Laoshigou, they took the stone on the Liu family land east of the ditch as City Boundary Marker No. 11. To Foyu, they took the left side of the stone stele cut stone, writing "Surface" on the left side with the gourd head as the boundary. They went to Longdong Temple again, taking the corner of the stone wall as City Boundary Marker No. 13, with the top of Songyu Pagoda as the boundary. A temporary meeting was held at Foyu, and it was decided that the next day it would be divided into two groups for demarcation. Group A would determine the boundary line between Daling and Xinglong Village. Group B would determine the boundary line between the watershed, Wenzhuang, and Huangling. They arrived at the Municipal Government at 8:00 AM. On the 14th, Hu Jingxi, Li Quanben, Zhao Jinming, and Huang Kui of Group A traveled south to Daling, taking the South Stone Cliff as City Boundary Marker No. 14, with the highest point of Daling as the boundary. To Xinglong Village, the stone pile under the large tree in front of the Guanyin Temple was taken as City Boundary Marker No. 16, with the pointed top of Pearl Mountain as the boundary. Li Weixia, Wu Chunyuan, and Ye Qi of Group B traveled southwest to the watershed, taking the Wang Qingyun stone wall south of the village as City Boundary Marker No. 17, with the South Mantou Mountain ridge as the boundary. To Wenzhuang, the Wang Lan stone dam south of the village was taken as City Boundary Marker No. 18. They went to Huangshanling again, taking the stone dam north of the main road as City Boundary Marker No. 19. Thus, the city and county boundary line was completed. It took five days, traveling about 300 li, and cost about 100 yuan.

Sections of the Guangshan Highway Completed 61

Status of Revenue from Traffic on Various Sections

Shantou Dispatch: The construction of the Guangshan Highway has been going on for three years, and the entire road is about to be completed. I asked the Eastern Road Highway Office yesterday about the conditions along the road. According to Director Zhang Youren, the total length of the Guangshan Road is about 1,000 li. The roadbed has been completed for 600 li, there are 100 cars, and 300 li of the road are passable, 300 li have been connected, 600 li of the roadbed have been newly built, and 350 li of the roadbed have been surveyed and are awaiting construction. The conditions of each section are described below:

First Trunk Provincial Road (1) Zhanghui Section (Zhangmutou to Huizhou): The three major bridges of Shima, Guancang, and Puzai, and more than ten other small bridges, are all built with reinforced concrete. The extended route connects to the Huiping section. It is faster to transport vehicles by boat, increasing vehicle speed by 2/10. Currently, it is jointly operated with the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway, with a 3/10 reduction in car prices and a 1/10 increase in revenue. (2) Huiping Section (Pingshan to Huizhou): The 140-foot Wutang Bridge has been built. From now on, all bridges on the road will be built with concrete. Recently, the route has been extended to connect to Huizhang Road, and a spacious station has been built near the city area, which has greatly increased passengers. (3) Pinghao Section (Pingshan to Haomen): About 140 li long, 40 li are open to traffic, with 10 cars. Except for the 40 li bandit area of Haomen, the rest is passable. Revenue for the year totaled 4,000 yuan, which is used for construction and management expenses. (4) Haohai Section (Haomen to Haifeng): About 50 li open to traffic. Except for the bandit area, it is all passable. The best roadbed, with a driving speed of 40 mph. In April of this year, the Daye Bridge was burned down by bandits. A three-in-one soil bridge is being rebuilt. The monthly income is about 1,000 yuan. (5) Hailu Section (Haifeng to Lufeng): The roadbed built since 1929 has been repeatedly repaired and transformed with concrete. The Hutiantian Bridge is 400 feet long, with 14 cars. The monthly income is about 8,000 yuan. (6) Lupu Section (Lufeng to Puning): This section starts from Bomei in Lufeng, which is the most prosperous coastline. There are 10 cars running, and the daily income is at most 30 to 40 yuan. Bomei to Kuitan also had a daily income of 20 to 30 yuan. Kuitan to Bengkan, Yunluo, Hanyan, and Chiwei have roughly the same income. The income from Chiwei to De'anli in Puning via Wushi is relatively small. The car company is located in Wushi, which suffered huge losses due to bandits. Traffic has now resumed. The bridge at Kuitan to Puning City is more than 100 miles long, and bandits are rampant, so attention should be paid to the bridges. The bridges at Huiping and Kuitan are all concrete, and the rest are mostly concrete beams to prevent them from being burned down by bandits. The recent losses due to bandits have been gradually repaired, costing several thousand yuan. The car company has been ordered to borrow money for repairs first. (7) Puji Section (Puning to Jieyang): It is 40 li long. The Jieyang section is the best. The Puning Guangtaiwei section has always had many bandits, and the nearby river management office opened the river, so it was not possible to send workers to build it. Near Jieyang City, only the north and south streams have not built wharves, and the bridges have not been directly connected to the Jie'an Road. (8) Jie'an Section (Jieyang to Chao'an): The Jieyang section has not yet been completed. The Chao'an section has been open to traffic for a long time. The bridges built several years ago have been severely damaged, and the roadbed is low and sunken, and it has not been filled in yet. The section near the border of the two counties has not yet been built. (9) Boxiang Section (Dongjiang Boluo to Lanshui): Completely new construction, already open to traffic. The daily income averages 40 to 50 yuan, and it is expected to develop in the future.

First Trunk Line of the Eastern Road: Bohui Section (Boluo to Huizhou): 43 li have been surveyed. Several li of the first branch line have been opened. (1) Puning to Shantou: 15 li from Chaoyang to Dazhao, 20 li from Heping, and 15 li from Jiaoshi to Leikou have been built. 35 li from Chaoyang to Hepingwei have been repaired. All of the above are open to traffic. (2) Chao'an to Huanggang: 3 li from Zhanglin to Jiuhe, and 2 li in the middle of Anzhai are open to traffic.

Second Trunk Line of the Eastern Road: The second trunk line had more than 100 li surveyed in September 1929. The Xinji Boluo to Heyuan is 40 li. Several miles are passable. The twenty miles along the river and forty miles on the south bank of the river from Heyuan to Longchuan are passable. Longchuan to Wuhua, Longchuan to Laolong, Qiling to Languan, and Dapu to Fengshi have been surveyed and are now under construction in order.

Report on Recent Administrative Policies of the Mongolian Committee 62

On the 18th, the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission sent specialist member Enhe Amur to the Central Radio Broadcasting Station to report on the recent administrative situation of the commission as follows: "Today, I am here on behalf of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission to give a report. There are four items to report. First, the facilities for Mongolian and Tibetan education. All undertakings in Mongolia and Tibet are backward, and the current shortcomings seem to be especially serious in education. Because education is not developed, there is no hope of progress in any matter. The central government also considers this very important. The Second National Education Conference in April of this year resolved to implement a plan for Mongolian and Tibetan education. The content of the plan is very thorough and detailed. In June of this year, when the central government convened the Mongolia-Gili Conference, the Ministry of Education sent the original plan to the commission and submitted it to the conference for discussion. The representatives of the various leagues and banners and the representatives of the governments of the border provinces unanimously agreed that it was feasible. The original plan has been approved and implemented in accordance with the planned procedures. The various levels of education in Mongolia and Tibet will definitely improve day by day. Once there is a solution for education, there will be no worries about talent. Therefore, all undertakings in Mongolia and Tibet can also gradually develop. However, for the past six months, wars have been frequent, and Mongolia and Tibet are far from Beijing. Although there is a very good plan, we still cannot actually implement it. This is something that the committee regrets. Now that the military affairs have ended and the country has been reunified, it is the duty of the commission to implement the plan step by step in order to develop Mongolian and Tibetan education. The Third Plenary Session of the Second Central Committee of the Party resolved to establish one Mongolian-Tibetan school in the capital and in suitable locations in Mongolia and Tibet to accommodate Mongolian and Tibetan youth, so that they can prepare for various subjects and serve as a reserve for training and construction personnel in Mongolia and Tibet, and to attach a Mongolian-Tibetan research class to specialize in researching, guiding, and promoting all matters in Mongolia and Tibet. Based on this resolution, the commission, together with the Ministry of Education, intends to establish one Mongolian-Tibetan school in the capital and Kangding. The organizational outlines of the two schools have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for promulgation. Once funds are available, they can be opened separately. Regarding the establishment of Mongolian-Tibetan classes attached to the Central Beijing Two Universities, since the commission circulated the news to Mongolia and Tibet, a total of sixty to seventy Mongolian and Tibetan students arrived this summer. Before entering the school, the commission provided all food and accommodation and contacted the Ministry of Education and Central University to open the class procedures. Only due to funding reasons, it is still difficult to establish the classes for a while. The committee believes that it is not easy for Mongolian and Tibetan students to travel thousands of miles to Beijing to study, and it is a pity to waste time. Therefore, the committee consulted with the Central Training Department to open a special class in the Central Political School, intending to name it the Mongolian-Tibetan Local Autonomy Class, to accommodate the Mongolian and Tibetan students who came to Beijing this time and cultivate Mongolian and Tibetan autonomous talents. However, the Mongolian-Tibetan class of Central University should still be urged to open as soon as possible, so that Mongolian and Tibetan students who continue to come to Beijing can enroll and study further. This is a point about education. Second, the committee has an office in Peiping, which has been suspended for the past six months due to various military and political reasons. Now that Peiping and Tianjin have been restored to their former appearance, the commission has appointed specialist member Ma neighboring area to take over and stationed the staff permanently in Peiping, responsible for reorganizing the office affairs. Third, the relationship between the central government and Tibet is now relatively close. The Dalai Lama previously sent Kunqiao Zhongni as a plenipotentiary representative to come to Beijing for engagement. At that time, Chairman Chiang was still at the front, and Chairman Ma of the commission accompanied Representative Kun to the front to meet the chairman. The results of the engagement were very satisfactory. According to Representative Kun, the Dalai also sent representatives to come to Beijing later. All matters concerning engagement between the central government and Tibet must be discussed when the representatives arrive in Beijing. Recently, the commission replies to every telegram it sends to the Dalai, and the Dalai also often sends telegrams on his own initiative, expressing his support for the central government. This is an unprecedented phenomenon in the twenty years since the founding of the Republic of China. Since the Dalai is sincerely inclined to the central government, there will soon be a considerable solution for the future of the central government and Tibet. Fourth, the commission had preparations last year to organize a new Mongolian and Tibetan Youth Investigation Group, intending to investigate the actual situation of new Mongolian and Tibetan youth as a basis for construction. However, due to repeated upheavals and traffic disruptions, it has not been implemented to this day. However, there are many foreign public and private organizations or individuals who are now going to Mongolia to carry out investigation work, but we do not have this organization to allow foreigners to wantonly dig and excavate, and even pack them away in boxes. This loss of antiquities is really detrimental to national sovereignty. Therefore, the commission regards the dispatch of personnel for investigation as very important. Now that the military affairs have ended, it is planned to continue the plan of last year and send personnel to Mongolia and Tibet for investigation as soon as possible."

Total Value of Agricultural and Mineral Products in Jiangsu Province 63

Reaching Over 3 Billion Yuan Annually

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining has always attached great importance to agricultural and mineral statistics. However, before the statistical work in various counties is sound and the weights and measures are unified, it is inevitable that there will be difficulties in the progress. Although agricultural investigators have been sent to various counties for field surveys, it is still difficult to obtain accurate and complete results for the time being due to various reasons. Recently, the department sent a letter to the Bureau of Industry and Commerce of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting the bureau to distribute the forms it had prepared to various counties to investigate the status of agricultural and mineral products. The counties have successively filled in the reports and the department has sorted them out. Although the content is very simple, it still has the value of an overview. The total value of agricultural and mineral products and by-products in the province is 3,194,526,533 yuan annually. Among them, agricultural products account for 75.11%, aquatic products account for 17.72%, forest products account for 0.85%, mineral products account for 0.88%, livestock and poultry and by-products account for 5.39%, and others account for 0.05%.

Soviet Russia Recruiting Troops in Harbin 64

Selecting from Overseas Chinese in the Eastern Provinces

Leaving a Unit to Guard the Russian Consulate

Harbin Correspondence: Soviet Russia recently sent personnel to Harbin to recruit new recruits for the National Defense Army from overseas Chinese. There are a total of five members of the recruitment committee, including three specialists sent by the Soviet Russian government, and the other two are appointed by the Consul General of Harbin, Melinigov, and the Consul General of Liaoning, Zinannisky, and appointed as chairman and vice-chairman. The recruitment committee office is located in the Russian Consulate in Harbin. According to the general practice of national defense, it is appropriate to inform the local government when recruiting troops from foreigners in the host country. However, the Russian consulate and others ignore the usual practice and implement it directly. Our side was completely unaware of it beforehand. Only because the authorities did not want to cause trouble, they allowed them to handle it freely. The recruitment method is to select pure Soviet Russian citizens residing in the Eastern Provinces, aged 18 to 40, with secondary education as qualified. Those who have already been enlisted are issued military uniforms. Therefore, in recent days, there are many Russians in military uniforms wandering in the streets of Harbin, and they run rampant in the city streets. The local police have no way to interfere. It is reported that the number of soldiers to be recruited in the Eastern Provinces is 2,500 in total. They have been sent back to the country in batches in recent days. Each batch has 40 to 50 people at most, and 20 to 30 people at least. Every time they board the train, all the Soviet Russian overseas Chinese in the city go to the station to see them off, and the situation is very enthusiastic. After the recruitment of these new recruits is completed, they will be trained in Chita. It is stipulated that they will be sent to the eastern border to be stationed in two months. The original National Defense Army will be transferred back to the western European border to be stationed. It is reported that in addition to sending most of the recruits back to their country, a small part will be left in plain clothes to guard the Russian consulates in Liaoning and Harbin. The total consulate is allotted 100 people, and the branch consulates are allotted 30 to 50 people. (11th)

Songjiang 65

Fire Drill Causes Misunderstanding: The Firefighting Association summoned a total of sixteen foreign water pumps and four pump trucks from the four districts of the city today (19th) to perform the drill in the open space of Caihua Jing as usual. Representatives from various agencies attended the scene to watch. Tang Renmei, the president of the association, and two others served as judges. In order to observe the firefighting performance of this session, a straw house was specially built, sprinkled with kerosene and ignited, so that each pump could rush to rescue, which was more grand than in previous sessions. Firefighting associations from various places in Shanghai's Second District, Qingpu, Jinshan, Xinbang and Fengjing all came to Songjiang in formation to watch. Unexpectedly, when the pump competition was halfway through, three members of the Dawang Temple used leather belts, exceeding the prescribed number of people, and were reported by members of the Sanxiu pump. The judges on the command platform immediately summoned the Dawang Temple pump members to report, in order to deduct points. However, the crowd was noisy and could not be summoned for a long time. The Sanxiu pump believed that the judges were unfair, and took off their copper hats and uniforms and threw them on the judging platform. Some people even removed the red board of the water spraying standard, and the order could not be maintained. It was announced that it would be stopped and resolved at a meeting.

Lüxiang Robbery Case: The Stolen Goods and Bandits Will Soon Be Brought to Justice: Fan Zicheng, the captain of the First Squadron of the Songjiang Water Police, immediately led the police to the scene after receiving the robbery alarm in Lüxiang. After jointly searching with the police of the whole county's Public Security Team, Liu Zhigao, the platoon leader stationed in Zhujing, and Lai, the army company commander, captured thirteen bandits, including Li Xiaoer and the monk Gengtai, from Dacheng An in the south corner of Lüxiang, and escorted them back to Zhujing for interrogation. On the 16th, three large packages of stolen goods, including 23 pieces of silk satin, Zhigong tweed, and leather clothing, were seized at Yao Laiyu's house in Nijiabang, Yucang. Yao was arrested and confessed without hesitation. The stolen goods were identified by the owners of Yao Jinmao and Ma Hengchang's shops as correct, and all were handed over to the court for handling. Now the military and police are still searching in separate ways according to the confessed hiding place of the bandits.

Wuxi 66

Details of the Strike at the Defeng Silk Factory: The Silk Factory Association of Xiyi previously held a general meeting of members at the County Chamber of Commerce on the Double Tenth Festival due to the tragic decline in the silk market and the difficulty for various factories to start reeling. It was decided on the spot to follow the example of various factories in Shanghai, and all wages of factory workers and employees would be paid at 80% from October to maintain the precarious situation. On the 15th of this month, the Defeng Silk Factory under Jinjun Bridge outside Nanmen implemented this decision when paying wages, and paid 80%. All the workers accepted it, but some employees refused to receive it. Unexpectedly, the next day (16th), some employees held a meeting behind Zhangwang Temple and decided to unite with the workers to implement a strike as a countermeasure. On the morning of the 17th, the factory rang the return sound as usual, and only half of the workers went to work. The rest of the female workers were wandering outside the factory, implementing a strike, and the order was very chaotic. Seeing that the factory had gone on strike and fearing that something would happen, the factory immediately called the third branch of the Public Security Bureau to send the police to suppress it to maintain order. At the same time, the Silk Factory Workers' Union, after hearing the news, sent Ding Shaochu to the factory to investigate and mediate, but the result was not satisfactory. Yesterday, the factory workers who joined the strike organized a strike committee and issued leaflets containing twelve requirements: (1) Oppose the expulsion of workers and friends, (2) Oppose the closure of the factory, (3) Wages will be paid as usual when the factory is closed, (4) Wages will be paid in full, and no reduction will be allowed, (5) No scolding of workers and friends is allowed, (6) Request to dismiss the chief steward Che Changmao, (7) Acknowledge that the strike committee has full representation of the workers to negotiate all strike matters, (8) Increase the wages of child laborers, (9) No work on Sundays, and wages will be paid as usual, (10) Oppose armed suppression of workers, (11) Implement an eight-hour work system, (12) Wages will be paid as usual during the strike period, and workers and friends shall not be dismissed on any pretext. On that day, the Silk Factory Association held a meeting, and Wang Kexing and Wang Rongshen, representatives of the Defeng Silk Factory, reported the process of the factory's strike. It was decided unanimously to provide assistance, and the representatives of the factory attending the meeting were notified to allow the extension of the shutdown period. If it is not resolved by November 15th, a countermeasure will be determined.

Silk Factory Industry Meeting Discusses Relief Issues: Shanghai and Wuxi silk factories have recently suspended operations one after another due to sluggish silk sales and inability to maintain business. The Shanghai Silk Factory Association convened representatives of silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Shanghai the day before yesterday to hold a relief conference. The representatives of the silk factories in this city who were dispatched to attend have returned to Wuxi from Shanghai, and a special 34th general meeting of members was convened yesterday afternoon to discuss relief issues. Representatives of 40 factories, including Xinlun, Minfeng, Yongfeng and Run, and 36 people, including Chen Fangquan, Fu Peide and Qin Shirong, attended. First, Qian, the chairman, reported the process of attending the relief conference in Shanghai. Then, they discussed the issues of borrowing public bonds and repayment methods. Zhang Zizhen expressed two opinions: (1) It is necessary for the factories in this city to borrow public bonds, which should be decided by each factory according to the situation. (2) The factories that borrow public bonds should follow the outline decided by the Jiangsu, Zhejiang and Shanghai Silk Industry Relief Special Committee, and levy a debt repayment fund of 20 taels of customs silver for each bundle of silk exported. If no public bonds are borrowed, there is no need to pay the debt repayment fund, as in the case of Shanghai Ewo and Suzhou Ruifeng. All the representatives agreed with this proposal and passed it unanimously. It was also decided to report this resolution at the second representative conference to be held in Shanghai on the 22nd. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Jiangyin 67

Jiang Hong Case Trial and Interrogation: Ji Shashi, the mother of Ji Hehua from Beiwai, sued Jiang Hong for suspicion of defrauding money. Yesterday (18th), the county government issued tickets to summon the related parties Mei Anlan, Yan Hongzhuang, Yin Zhongren, and Chen Zhongda for interrogation. None of Mei and others appeared in court, only submitting statements. The investigation court was opened at 4 pm, and the plaintiff Ji Shashi was present. Jiang Hong was interrogated by Yang Cheng. According to Ji Shashi, around July 6th of the lunar calendar, Jiang Hong came to my house and said that he was a friend of his son Hehua and tried to help him, but money was necessary, and he wanted 5,000 yuan, saying that he had contacted Mei Anlan. At Zhang Jingying's house on Dongda Street, I agreed to 3,000, Mei said 4,000, and then added 1,000, not in cash, but all Chengfeng Zhuang bills, which were paid to him around the middle of July in the lunar calendar. Later, he exchanged 2,000 in cash, 1,000 in banknotes, and 1,000 in Zhuang bills. Jiang promised that Hehua would be released from prison in about three days. Around August 8th of the lunar calendar, Jiang said that Hehua could be released on bail. She waited for a day, but there was no news. The next day, she went to Zhang's house to ask Anlan Hongzhuang, and Jiang also came. He said that he wanted Hehua to admit some communist incidents and write a sentence. When she heard about it, she knew that Jiang was cheating her, and went home and cried bitterly at the back door, wanting to drown herself. He said that the 5,000 yuan was for expenses, and he would open an account with her after Hehua was released from prison, and did not explain what the expenses were. Jiang Hong said that Ji Shashi's statement was completely inconsistent with the facts. I did not go to Ji's house. Ji Shashi often came to the Southeast Rural Society to see me, asking me to find a way to rescue Hehua, and even came to my house in the rain in the month (Xiachang Zhao Chun), and the sedan chair bearers, one named Zhang and one named Li, can be called as witnesses. She wanted to send me 1,000 yuan in banknotes, and I refused. Later, her husband Chengyu, Mei Anlan, and Hongzhuang came to say that Hehua's family was willing to donate 10,000 yuan to purchase guns for the local area. I told the county magistrate about it, but he did not agree. Later, I told Li, the director of the Public Security Bureau, to the county magistrate, but he also did not agree. His family had requested it in writing, but it was also rejected. Mei and others asked me to help, and gave me 5,000 yuan in Zhuang bills. 2,000 yuan was donated to the relief home, and 3,000 yuan was used for local gun management, entrusting me to keep it. When Hehua is released from prison, he will write a donation slip. I also told Meng Yaping, a member of the party department, about this matter, but he did not say yes or no. The Hong Ji account on the bill is that the 2,000 yuan deposited in the relief home has been used up. It is deposited under a private name, and 100 yuan was deposited for the food expenses of the medical center. Because it happened to be the Mid-Autumn Festival, the director Wang Gengjun urgently wanted to pay it. He had requested the county magistrate, thinking that the 2,000 yuan donation could be used. However, after this was preserved, there was no way to release Hehua. The day before yesterday (4th), while eating wine at Huachang, I discussed the method with Yin Zhongren, Li Gong, Director of the Bureau, and Wang Guanqin. I wholeheartedly confessed, and now I am suffering for others, and I only hate my excessive enthusiasm. Please the court to call Mei Anlan and others as witnesses. When Jiang Hong was giving his statement, Ji Shashi denied hiring a sedan chair to Jiang's house at Yueqiao. After a fierce debate, Ji Shashi wiped her tears frequently with a towel, showing her eagerness to protect her son. The interrogation took a long time. The court ordered Mei Anlan and others to be summoned to court for interrogation, and at the same time to conduct a detailed investigation of the facts before reviewing the case. Ji Shashi was handed over to the original guarantor, and Jiang Hong was taken back into custody.

Nantong 68

Salt Reclamation Police Corps Established: The coastal salt reclamation area of ​​Jiangbei has suffered great losses due to the harassment of bandits. It has been approved by the provincial government to organize a self-defense police corps, with Xiong Yanghe, the captain of the Funing County Police Team, concurrently serving as the commander. The guns, equipment and other items cost a total of 40,000 yuan, and the regular expenses are set at 30,000 yuan per year, which is shared by various companies. The corps has now been formed and is stationed in the reclamation area for security.

Expansion of Detention Center Implemented: The Nantong County Court believes that the detention center is too crowded with prisoners, and has obtained approval from the High Court to raise donations for expansion. A certain amount has now been donated, and nearby real estate has been purchased to rebuild the prison building.

Gaoyou 69

Fanzhuang Steamer Robbed: The short-haul steamer from Shaobo to Fanzhuang of Dada Company was attacked by five boats and more than 40 bandits with guns at Qiusujiao at 4 pm the day before yesterday. The captain of the steamer, fearing that the passengers would be injured, stopped the boat immediately. The bandits swarmed aboard and looted, and none of the passengers were spared. It is said that the losses were huge. At that time, a helping boat from Shaobo to Xinghua also encountered the bandits and was looted.

Kidnappers Escorted to Suzhou for Trial: The police team of this county arrested three kidnappers, Di Guangren, Xia Dakouzi, and Qiao Naihe, a month ago. They have been sentenced to imprisonment by Hu Cheng, the trial judge. The bandits refused to accept the sentence and filed an appeal. Now that the date of the appeal trial is approaching, the three criminals were shackled and escorted to the Suzhou High Court for trial this morning.

After confirming their confessions, they were sentenced to death and approved by the provincial government. On the morning of the 16th at 11:00 am, the criminals were tied to the execution ground and executed by firing squad.

Ma Yuren's Troops Fled to Juegang: After being severely attacked by the provincial security regiment, Ma Yuren's troops, who were entrenched in Yancheng and Funing, had more than 30 bandit ships fleeing to Juegang, and parked in the ports of Shayu Wanzai and Cheling, carrying out ship robbery. Yesterday (15th), three fishing boats were robbed and two fishing boats were burned, and they threatened to land and loot the whole town. Now the people in the area are extremely panicked and uneasy.

Changshu 71

Telephone Dispute Resolved: The local Electricity and Gas Users Association and the telephone company had a dispute over the price increase issue, and each took extreme measures, which have not been resolved. Recently, County Magistrate Tan and Zhang, Director of the Telegraph Bureau, have persuaded and mediated, and made every effort to mediate. Yesterday, an agreement was reached in the county government to collect the monthly fee from November of the 19th year according to the original numbers of 5 yuan for Type A and 6 yuan for Type B. No further increase will be made within two years from July of this year. Both parties signed an agreement and the four-month dispute has been completely resolved.

Hang, Commander of Hangzhou, Transferred to Director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau: Hang Yi, the commander of the Jiahu Bandit Suppression Command, was ordered to be transferred to the Director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau. Therefore, Commander Hang has completed the bandit suppression affairs and is waiting for the handover. According to inside sources, after Hang is transferred, the province plans to abolish the Bandit Suppression Command, and the First and Second Guerrilla Teams under his command will be directly commanded by the provincial government. The bandit suppression affairs in Jiahu County will be the responsibility of the Security Team. Shangyu 73

Security Team Arrests Opium Traffickers: Zhangzhen in this county is an important road to Sheng County. Recently, due to the rampant bandits in the county, Zhangzhen has been under martial law for days. Ships passing through must be inspected before they are allowed to pass. At around 9 pm the night before last, a private boat from Baiguan to Sheng County was passing through the defense zone. There were two young women from Sheng County as passengers, carrying a large amount of opium. They were found by the soldiers of the Security Team and taken with the goods to the 11th Company Headquarters of the 3rd Battalion of the 6th Regiment, and temporarily detained overnight. The next day, they were escorted to the Baiguan Regiment Headquarters for disposal.

Education News

Important News 75

Meeting Record of the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Teachers' Association

The Jiangsu Provincial Joint Association of Teachers and Staff of Provincial Middle Schools held its seventh representative conference at Zhenjiang Middle School on October 12th and 13th. A total of 17 schools attended, including Sun Tingsheng from Shangzhong, Zheng Baozi from Taizhong, Liu Xianqi from Ruzhong, Liu Suisheng from Songzhong (also representing Song Girls' Middle School), Xue Xuyun from Changzhong, Wang Shoukang from Xuzhong (representing), Qian Xiuzhi from Huaiyin Middle School, Huang Xinyun from Huaian Middle School, Xue Jianwu from Tongzhong, Si Jianan from Huaiyin Agriculture, Zhang Zhongyou from Xizhong, Wu Cangsu and Li Chonghu from Yangzhong, Huang Zemin from Su Girls' Middle School, Tu Gangzhi from Su Girls' Sericulture, and Wang Dagang and Shen Wenmei from Suzhong (also representing Su Agriculture), as well as five former executive committee members Xue Tianyou, Zhang Shaonan, Huang Zemin, Zhang Zhongyou, and Sun Tingsheng. A total of 25 proposals were discussed at this conference, among which the most important ones are approximately five points: (1) Publish "Jiangsu Secondary Education Review" (semi-monthly) to devote all efforts to publicity and criticism with keen eyes and fair attitudes, so that people across the country can understand the truth of secondary education in Jiangsu, in order to make positive contributions, and avoid the previous passive methods such as submitting requests to government offices. Starting from November of this year, each school will take turns in editing. (2) Focus on teaching research, and hold a Chinese language subject research conference at Yangzhou Middle School on December 1st. Before the end of March next year, collect specific opinions from various schools on the middle school curriculum standards promulgated by the ministry, in order to submit them to the Ministry of Education for revision, and urge all members to selectively compile applicable middle school textbooks. (3) Suggestions for reorganizing education funding: (1) Request the provincial department to strictly pursue the education funding arrears of various counties in accordance with the County Magistrate Performance Evaluation Regulations. (2) Request the Education Funding Committee to move the management office to Zhenjiang and appoint an accountant to clear the accounts of previous years. (3) Request the provincial government to revise the Education Funding Committee's organizational law and add one representative from this association. (4) Request the Department of Education to limit the management office to clear the arrears of the three months of July, August, and September of this year by the end of October. If there is no effect, all members will make a serious expression. (4) Assistance in the Xiao Case: Request the Department of Education to consult the military and political authorities to investigate the incident of Mr. Xiao Mingqin being insulted, and be able to order local troops to be responsible for the protection of education personnel at any time. (5) Organize domestic and foreign education observation groups. The remaining cases are not recorded.

Lehua Was Overwhelmed by Huasais as Soon as They Played 80

—Their strength is far inferior to before—They suffered a defeat of one to five—

Lehua Football Team lost to Huasais by a score of one to five in the Westerners' League A yesterday. Huasais last year, although as strong as today, was not an opponent of Lehua. Now that the times have changed and the environment is different, those who have lost have turned to worship. When I think of those years, I can't help but sigh.

(1) Spectators Were Like Clouds 81

Lehua's fame has long been soaring in Shanghai. Although the veterans have been scattered and the strength has been greatly damaged, the talents recruited are also of good reputation. Therefore, Shanghai fans are eager to know what Lehua's strength is today compared with previous years. The road to Father Lao was crowded and bustling. Inside the China Baseball Stadium, there were mountains of people, and the number was the highest ever in this session.

(2) Interest Is Greatly Reduced 82

Lehua's performance on that day was disappointing. Only Li Huitang was still as good as ever. The work of passing and shooting was indeed worthy of appreciation. The rest was mediocre. The whole team's organization was at the beginning, and the individuality could not be mutually understood. Li Ning, Chen Yutian and others did not participate. How can we achieve the effect of unified arms? Therefore, the forward attack was without any steps, and the defense inside was stable. Within 90 minutes, they were oppressed by the enemy. Occasionally breaking the encirclement, it is difficult to show prestige in a foreign land. If there was no Li Huitang with special skills to hit a ball, wouldn't the whole army be annihilated? Viewers were greatly reduced to this point of interest.

(3) Two Teams 83

Hua Sai Si (Wales)

Luan Tuo (Lewis) Ha He Si (Hughes)

Ai Ya Deng (Airden) Zhong Bo (Chambers)

Fei Lie Pi Si (Phillips) Huo Ting Xun (Hodgson) Bo Te (Brett)

Bao Tuo (Boughton) Xu Er (Hulse)

Le Hua Team

Jin Feng De (Kim Bong Deok) Wang Ji Huai (Wang Jihuai)

Qian Yao Bin (Qian Yaobin) Cui Dong Xian (Choi Donghyeon)

Lu Zhong En (Lu Zhongen) Zhang Xu Long (Zhang Xulong) Li Hui Tang (Li Huitang)

Gao Da Han (Gao Dahan) Xi Qiao Sheng (Xi Qiaosheng)

An Yuan Sheng (An Yuansheng) (Captain) Yang Ren Wei (Yang Renwei)

(4) The Goal Wide Open 84

Referee Lei Tai blew his silver whistle, and the two teams deployed their formations. Soon, the fierce battle began. First, Hua Sai Si launched an invasion, and Le Hua resisted from all sides. Finally, An Yuan Sheng led the escape from danger. Li Hui Tang passed the ball with his head, and Yang Ren Wei greeted and sent it to the center, forcing a corner kick, which was ineffective. Hua Sai Si attacked again, deeply penetrating the heart of Le Hua's defense, but their entire effort was wasted due to an offside on the left wing. At that time, Le Hua's morale was high, and their attack and defense were both fierce and imposing. In the blink of an eye, Li Hui Tang cleverly evaded and provided a good opportunity for Xi Qiao Sheng to attack, but the shot was too weak and was saved by the goalkeeper. Li then used his lively movements, roaming across the left area, unexpectedly picked a pass to the front of the goal. The goalkeeper and inside defender were unable to turn around in time, and the goal was wide open. Xi Qiao Sheng moved forward, met the ball with his head, and with a loud thud, it crossed the goal line. The audience, after their disappointment, could only force a wry smile.

(5) Great Merit 85

Le Hua launched several attacks, but none hit the enemy's vital points, and the vigor of their forwards was almost completely exhausted. Fortunately, the defense of the backs was still able to fulfill its duty. Lu Zhong En, alone, blocked the enemy's charge, falling to the ground to save the ball, and succeeded. His merit was great. The danger was not over, and the enemy invaded from the left again, shooting fiercely at the goal. Lu raised a single palm to catch it, once again escaping danger. Then the enemy shot a ball from the ground, with great momentum. Lu bent down to block it, again ensuring safety.

(6) Greatly Reduced Vitality 86

After twenty minutes, Le Hua's resistance gradually weakened. The greatest hidden danger was their internal disarray, scattered or gathered, with no order. At that time, a ball came from the left, and the two inside defenders were at a loss, each using their bodies to block the advance of the left and right inside forwards. Lu Zhong En took the opportunity to come forward and steal the ball, but suddenly collided and fell to the ground. The right inside forward Xu Er added a foot and hit the ball into the goal. Within two minutes, the right winger Mai Lie Tai lofted a high ball. The strong wind carried the ball, swirling in the air, and the inside defenders did not know what to do. The center forward Bo Te shot another ball into the goal. Le Hua lost two goals in a row and became greatly enraged. Xi Qiao Sheng got another chance to shoot, but it was caught by the goalkeeper. Cui Yang charged fiercely, and the goalkeeper fell to the ground, but still held on tightly. Finally, relying on his strong body, he broke through the encirclement and escaped danger. But Hua Sai Si's forwards went straight in, winning two corner kicks in a row. As a result of the second corner kick, center forward Bo Te again hit the ball into the net. By this time, Hua Sai Si had won three goals, while Le Hua had none.

(7) Quick Action 87

Since Le Hua had lost ground, they were determined to regain it. At the start of the second half, Le Hua changed their formation, as shown in the previous table. At that moment, Hua Sai Si was dazzled by the shifting formations, and the situation was slightly chaotic. Li Hui Tang emerged as a surprise force, assisting Xi Qiao Sheng in their advance. When the opportunity arrived, they immediately attacked the goal, with great momentum and strength. The goalkeeper could not block it, and the ball still went into the goal past the post. With one goal scored, their morale was greatly boosted. Ten minutes later, Le Hua encountered another good opportunity. Li and Yang both approached the enemy's goal, but unfortunately, they hindered each other, making it difficult to shoot. Otherwise, there would have been another amazing move.

(8) A Disorganized Mess 88

From then on, Hua Sai Si's activity suddenly increased. The front army won victory after victory, with irresistible force. Le Hua's internal organization was like a disorganized mess, beyond repair. In the last ten minutes, they lost two more goals in a row, one scored by the center forward and one by the left inside forward. The latter goal was clear and beautiful, truly worthy of praise. At the end of the battle, Hua Sai Si won with a score of five to one.

Chinese Football Club's Match: Lingnan Defeats Baota 90

Result: Six to Two

The Lingnan Football Team in the "Zhong" Group of the Chinese Football Club can also be called a strong team. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, they competed against Baota in the "Zuo" Group at the Chinese Football Field. The referee was Tang Zhong Guang.

Lingnan was strong both internally and externally, gaining an upper hand. Chen Hong Guang opened the scoring, and Liang Min Fa followed, scoring the second goal. Under pressure, Baota launched fierce attacks, but retreated unfavorably because the opposing formation was well-organized. Baota lost the first half with a score of 0-2.

In the second half, Lingnan, with its rich experience, had already discovered the opponent's weaknesses. They seized the opportunity to attack and achieved their desires. Baota defended key positions and tried hard to resist, but they were too weak and unable to defend everywhere. Soon, Chen Hong Guang scored the third goal, and Zhuo Guo Rong added another goal. Chen then scored another goal. Baota, after conceding five goals, became enraged. The forward line surged in like a tide. Lingnan was momentarily careless and accidentally kicked the ball into their own goal. But before long, Liang Min Fa again showed his skills and scored another goal. In a counter-attack, Baota had the opportunity for a penalty kick, but they did not score directly. However, Wang Zhang Bao also regained a goal as a result, making the result two to six. Victory went to Lingnan.
