Keio Again Defeats Waseda 95

—Result: Five to Four—

—Ticket Rush Occurs—

—The Audience is Very Lively—

Tokyo, Electric Communication on the 19th. The second Keio-Waseda match was very lively. The game started at 2:00 PM today with Keio batting first. Keio's pitcher was Ueno, and the catcher was Ogawa. Waseda used Ito as the pitcher, with Miura guarding the home plate, preparing for Keio's strong hitters. In the first inning, Waseda scored one point first, gaining the upper hand. Keio got a chance in the first half of the second inning, scoring two points, reversing the situation and winning by one point. In the third and fourth innings, both sides did not score, fighting fiercely. In the first half of the fifth inning, Keio scored another point. In the second half of this inning, when Waseda was attacking, Keio replaced Ueno with Mizuhara to restrain Waseda. In the sixth inning, Waseda also sent Ito away, replacing him with Tashiro Ogawa. Neither team scored in the sixth inning. In the first half of the seventh inning, Keio scored another point. Waseda replaced Ogawa, and Tasei came on from the middle. In the second half of this inning, when Waseda attacked, Keio changed the pitcher to Miyatake and the catcher to Okada, refreshing their formation. Waseda failed to score. By this inning, the score was four to one. Although Waseda's situation was unfavorable, in the second half of the eighth inning, they still launched a desperate attack, breaking through Miyatake's fierce ball and scoring three points in one fell swoop, making the score a tie of four to four. The entire stadium stood up and shouted wildly. Only a small number of Waseda supporters danced in disorder. In the last ninth inning, Keio seized the opportunity to cleverly score one point. Waseda sent a support batter to pursue, but it was ineffective. Finally, Keio won again with a score of five to four, singing victory songs. The game ended at 4:30 PM. The referees were Qian Cun (ball), Yokozawa, and Tenchi (base). The results of the battle are as follows:

Keio 0 2 0 0 1 0 1 0 1 5

1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8 9

Waseda 1 0 0 0 0 0 3 0 4

Tokyo, Electric Communication on the 19th. Due to the ticket issue for the Keio-Waseda match, the dispute between Waseda University and the students suddenly turned into a purely student disturbance around the time the Keio-Waseda match began yesterday afternoon. When the game at the Meiji Jingu Stadium was in full swing, and the entire city was in a state of frenzy, the entire Waseda United Student Committee was holding a general assembly at the Okuma Auditorium in Waseda University, with successive speeches, and the atmosphere was high. At 5:30 PM, the entire audience unanimously decided to publish the following articles:

1. Recognize the entire Waseda United Student Committee.

2. Deny the Athletic Association and order its immediate dissolution.

3. Those responsible for this incident must apologize.

4. Explain the reason for the temporary holiday on the 18th.

5. Absolutely oppose the illegal punishment by the school authorities.

The school is holding an emergency meeting to request countermeasures. Last night, they rejected the committee's request for a meeting. This morning at 9:00 AM, they will hold another faculty meeting to request a proper settlement. The school's attitude seems to be quite firm. The root cause of this dispute is that since the military education incident the year before last, the students' autonomy has been suddenly reduced. The students' dissatisfaction with the school authorities has been brewing for a long time. The ticket incident triggered the outbreak. The undergraduate department, higher academy, specialized department, and normal school, totaling 13,000 students who had no contact mechanism, immediately elected class committees to organize the entire Waseda Student United Committee to confront the school. The strategy of boycotting tickets was successful. The dissatisfaction with the school authorities suddenly erupted, turning a mere ticket incident into a major issue.

Northeast Four Provinces Joint Games (1) 96

Detailed Record of the First Day

Shenyang Communication. The first Northeast United Games opened on the 11th at the newly built sports field of Northeastern University in Beiling. President Zhang Xueliang personally attended the venue to give words of encouragement. 96 groups participated in the competition, with 1,060 male and female athletes and more than 20,000 spectators. Here is a detailed record of the various situations on the first day.

A Glimpse of the Venue The venue is in the Northeastern University Stadium, which was built with a donation of 400,000 yuan from Zhang Hanqing. Construction lasted for a year and has now been completed. It was designed and built by the Jietai Construction Company, which is most famous in North China. Everything is very scientific. There is a long arc-shaped grandstand on the northeast three sides, stretching for two li. When the North China Games were held in Shenyang last year, as well as the Sino-Japanese-German competition, they were all held here, but at that time the field was not fully repaired. Now it is completely new, solemn and grand. On the east and west sides of the field, there are president's platforms. The decoration of the west platform is even better than the east platform. The opening ceremony of the conference was held on the west platform. In addition, the audience grandstand has 12 levels, each level is represented by a character, from bottom to top, according to the Heavenly Stems and Earthly Branches (Zi, Chou, Yin, Mao, Chen, Si, Wu, Wei, Shen, You, Xu, Hai). Each seat is numbered separately. Due to the large number of guests, seats were not arranged according to the numbers. There are 15 entrances to the field. The door frame is marked with a thousand characters, from "Tian" to "Lie." The door under the west chairman's platform is the "Xuan" character door. In order to maintain order in the venue, the conference organizing committee stamped the character marked on the door on the admission ticket and entered according to the character. In addition, two Boy Scouts were assigned to each gate to be responsible for checking tickets to prevent confusion, so the order on the grandstand was excellent. A wooden clock is hung directly north of the platform, with a diameter of about two feet. The hour and minute hands are three inches thick. All high and low places throughout the venue are clearly visible. The clock is manually operated by a Boy Scout, who is responsible for moving it every ten minutes, which is a perfect method. On this day, from about 6:00 AM, various primary and secondary schools in the city arrived in groups.

Opening Ceremony At 9:00 AM, Zhang Xueliang and his wife Yu Fengzhi arrived at the venue and the meeting began. The players of each team stood under the chairman's platform. The master of ceremonies called to play music and raise the flag. The flagpole was set up in the southern part of the field. In the gentle breeze, the bright blue and white flag slowly rose. Then, all the people present, led by Deputy Commander Zhang, bowed three times to the flag of the party and the country. After the ceremony, Zhang Xueliang respectfully read the Premier's will and sang the party song. Then, the chairman of the organizing committee gave a report, briefly stating that the conference was held with the support of Deputy Commander Zhang and various circles. All expenses were borne by Deputy Commander Zhang personally and the Hanqing Education Foundation Committee. He expressed his deep gratitude. However, in terms of expenses, he tried his best to be thrifty. There are currently 96 participating groups and 51 competition items. As for the competition rules and order in the venue, President Wang will report again, etc. Then Wang Hua Yi reported, briefly stating that after the closing of this conference, he will proceed to organize a (Northeast Sports Association).

President's Speech Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, carrying his wife, attended the venue and gave a speech, saying, "Dear teachers, staff, and players, participating in today's grand event, more than a thousand athletes gathered in one place, showing the spirit of youth in competition. Therefore, I would like to say a few words. The pain of the failure of the last Far East Games, and the fluke of the national sports in the Northeast, have been described in detail by President Wang Hua Yi. Today, the best results created by our country's athletes cannot only be maintained permanently, but are shrinking daily. This is even more important than actual failure. There are many reasons for this, but in a nutshell, it is a lack of training. Other things, such as the society's excessive praise of athletes, are also enough to cultivate athletes' vanity and laziness. You must know that athletes engage in sports not for what they hope to gain, as do those who do business. Moreover, sports honor is public, not personal. Therefore, all players must broaden their horizons. Even speaking of this conference, this is the first one. There are still the second and third sessions to come. If we fail this time, we can still compete for victory another day. Even if we win this time, we still have to compare with the whole country. If the whole country wins, we still have to participate in the Far East Games and other events. The future is bright. Without hard work and training, it is difficult to achieve the final effect. Flukes cannot succeed permanently, and failure is not permanent failure. I hope all players will remember this and not forget it."

Oath Parade After the President's speech, the sports oath was taken. The text said, "(I solemnly swear to abide by the competition rules, obey the referees, and maintain sportsmanship with amateur sports qualifications.)" Then there was a parade.

Athletes from various places (A) Middle School Group for Men: Liaoning 56, Jilin 48, East Special 39, Heilongjiang 47, (B) Middle School Group for Women: Liaoning 80, Jilin 36, East Special 19, Heilongjiang 10, (C) High School Group for Men: Liaoning 81, Jilin 17, East Special 15, Dalian 9, Individual participants 8, (D) High School Group for Women: Liaoning 26, Jilin 5, East Special 5.

City No. 1 Stadium Athletic Sports Meet 98

The City No. 1 Public Stadium Athletic Sports Meet began at 8:00 AM yesterday and ended at 4:00 PM. Due to thunderstorms the night before, the ground was slightly wet in the morning, and some athletes failed to participate on schedule. But after 9:00 AM, the sun appeared and the weather cleared, and the sports field was neither dry nor wet, making it ideal for competition. Therefore, the players were full of energy and competed to be the first to reach the top. Here is a record of the situation:

Opening Ceremony At 8:00 AM, the bell rang for the opening ceremony. The president, referees, staff, and athletes gathered in front of the chairman's platform and performed the rituals. President Wang Zhuangfei delivered the opening speech, briefly stating that he welcomed everyone who participated in the conference and came to compete in their spare time. The purpose of this conference is to showcase everyone's achievements, attract the attention of the general public, and encourage them to practice sports and exercise their bodies, and to prove the depth of everyone's daily training and the extent of their physical fitness. From now on, we will increase our interest and continue to practice to reach the highest standards. I hope that everyone will compete with the spirit of amateur sports and will be able to implement this purpose.

Spectators There were fewer spectators in the morning, about 700 or 800 people. In the afternoon, the number gradually increased to 2,000 or 3,000 people. When there were long-distance races, they often cheered to boost the spirits of the runners, and the interest was particularly strong. The order of the venue was maintained by the Boy Scouts of the East Asia Sports School, and it was well-organized.

Track and Field Events None of the famous athletes participated in this sports meet, giving the opportunity to new athletes to win the championship. The intention was excellent. Therefore, although the results of the competition failed to create special records, the large number of participants and the full spirit of the competition were also indelible achievements. It is a pity that in the 400-meter final in the afternoon, Guan Changfa suddenly moved diagonally to the outer lane midway, obstructing the progress of the person behind him. After the inspector reported to the chief referee, his results were cancelled. The procedure was completely in compliance. Unexpectedly, Guan Changfa was a member of the Baihong team, and more than a dozen members of the same team, acting on impulse, wanted to withdraw from the sports meet, and even the finish line referee Song Zean left at the same time due to his relationship with the Baihong team members, which was a pity. <Civilian Warship Planning Completed P]> Awaiting the Launch of the Yixian Warship Before Construction Begins The Ministry of the Navy ordered the Jiangnan Shipyard in this port to build the Yixian warship. The hull is nearing completion and the launch ceremony is scheduled for the 12th of next month, coinciding with the Prime Minister's birthday. As for the Minsheng warship to be built after the Yixian, the Jiangnan Shipyard has already drawn up plans and submitted them to the Ministry for approval. The naval vessel supervision and construction department was instructed to commence construction a few days ago. The ship is planned to be 204 feet long, 26 feet wide, 11 feet 8 inches high, with a draft of 6 inches, a speed of 18 miles, and an armament of nine cannons, including one 4.7-inch bow gun, one 3-inch stern gun, two 6-pound side guns, four light machine guns, and one anti-aircraft gun. The crew will consist of 304 people, and the launch is scheduled for the Double Tenth Festival of the 20th year [of the Republic]. The Provincial Office Orders the Suppression of Illegal Farmers' Organizations The Shanghai County Government received an order from the Jiangsu Agricultural and Mining Office, stating that, in order to comply with the matter, the Agricultural and Mining Department issued an order stating that the organizational plan for people's groups, as passed by the Second Plenary Session, stipulates that people's groups are divided into professional groups and social groups, and the organizational procedures have been promulgated by the National Government. It is now based on the rural survey forms filled out by various provinces, which include the organization of farmers' groups with various names such as the God Society, Sacrifice Society, Revolutionary Group, Three People's Principles Group, Renovation Group, Red Society, Yellow Society, Red and White Spears Society, and Sitting and Mountain Walking Groups. Since these organizations are freely organized without following the procedures stipulated by the central government, it is inevitable that there are unscrupulous elements within them. Their impact on rural areas is not insignificant. In addition to separate orders, the office urgently orders the bureau to instruct its subordinates that if there are organizations similar to the above, they should immediately, together with the local party headquarters, conduct detailed investigations and suppress them separately, and report the suppression situation for future reference. It is of utmost importance. The county magistrate is hereby ordered to immediately cooperate with the local party headquarters to implement the above, and to report the implementation situation for verification and transfer. Trade Associations Support the Implementation of Industry Regulations Meeting To Nominate Drafters for Drafting Dozens of trade associations, including the Seven Cities Intestine Industry, Bamboo Industry, Pharmaceutical Industry, Paper Industry, and Fresh Ice Industry, believe that the industry regulations approved for registration by the trade associations should be universally followed by all businesses in the industry, whether they are members of the association or not. Only in this way can the provisions of Article 2 of the Trade Association Law promulgated by the central government, which seek the common interests of the industry and correct industry malpractices, be effectively implemented. They gathered yesterday to discuss the matter and nominated drafters to prepare a draft to be submitted to the National Government. After further scheduled approval, it will be issued. Notice Soliciting Donations for the Family of Hu Bingxu The Shanghai Bar Association issued a notice to all members yesterday, stating that it received a letter from the family of the late Judge Hu Bingxu (also known as Tefu) of the Jiangsu Higher Court, stating that Mr. Hu served as a judicial officer with integrity that was known to all. He was diligent to the point of illness. Now that he has passed away, his family is impoverished. It is difficult to bury him in his hometown, and his family is finding it difficult to make ends meet. He left behind a widow and young children, and although they have received assistance from superiors and colleagues, it is not enough. They are appealing to all, whether they are close friends or simply admire his integrity, to show compassion and offer assistance. The letter includes a eulogy detailing Mr. Hu's integrity and dedication to justice during his life, which was admired by colleagues in both Shanghai and Jiangsu. His sudden passing is deeply regretted, and his family is in dire straits. It is appropriate to offer financial assistance. Therefore, the eulogy is enclosed and sent to all members, with the hope that they will generously contribute to help those in need. Donations should be sent to the association before November 15th. (The rest is omitted) The Crime of Soliciting Lawsuits, Fraud, and Attempted Acquisition of Property Zhang Zuotang Sentenced to Six Months of Imprisonment Zhang Zuochang, an assistant to lawyer Feng Kan at 600 North Shaanxi Road, repeatedly used the name of lawyer Zhang Guisan on April 7th, 8th, 15th, and 17th to demand payment of 370 taels of silver from Gongchang Embroidery Shop at 1259 Zhongde Lane, Beijing Road, on behalf of Yuanshun Seafood Shop. He then, in his capacity as the legal representative of Yuanshun Shop, filed a lawsuit against Gongchang Shop in the civil court of the Special District. After the court issued a summons, Yuanshun suddenly refused to accept it, stating that the shop had not engaged in any litigation with Gongchang. On June 16th and July 5th, the court held hearings. Zhang initially appeared in court under the name of Zhang Zuotang, then under his own name, and later under the name of lawyer Zhang Guisan. The Shanghai Bar Association learned of this and reported to Chief Prosecutor Zhou Xianjue of the Special Court, as there was no lawyer Zhang Guisan in the association. Zhou ordered lawyer Zhou Rubao Yi of the Public Works Department to investigate, and after obtaining substantial evidence, filed a public prosecution accusing Zhang of impersonating a lawyer and attempting to acquire property through fraud, a crime under Article 363, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law. After several hearings by the Special Court, Zhang Zuotang claimed that Zhang Guisan was a Hangzhou lawyer and that he had a liaison office at his house and could represent all matters. The court ordered Zhang to pay 500 yuan bail to be released pending investigation and further hearings. Subsequently, the Special Court received a letter from a Hangzhou lawyer stating that he had not entrusted Zhang Zuotang to represent all matters. The case has been concluded by the court, and lawyer Ru requested that Zhang be severely punished. The judgment was announced yesterday morning by Judge Zhou in the first criminal court. The main text stated that Zhang Zuotang was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of soliciting lawsuits, fraud, and attempted acquisition of property. If the defendant is not satisfied with the judgment, he must file an appeal. Judge Zhou then ordered Zhang Zuotang to pay 700 yuan bail during the appeal period and await summons from the Court of Appeal. A Quarrel Between a Laborer and a Carpenter A Knife Wound to the Back Zhou Changan, a 22-year-old from Yangzhou, residing at 984 Huimin Yarn Factory, Yangshupu, was carrying tiles at the Shanghai Fifth Yarn Factory in Yangshupu around 10:00 yesterday morning when he had a quarrel with a carpenter. He was stabbed in the back with a knife by the carpenter, fell to the ground, and bled profusely. He was later sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by Constable Zhou. Qianlong's Tour of Jiangnan Accusation of Unauthorized Screening The Order to Reschedule the Retrial Tianyi Film Company rented the first, second, and third episodes of "Qianlong's Tour of Jiangnan" to Lin Lübing of Fujian in December of last year. The lease stipulated a period of sixty days. After the expiration, Lin colluded with Xu Daoyu of the Fuzhou Dahua Company to screen the films in various parts of Fujian Province without authorization. Upon hearing this, the company sent personnel to Fujian and found that the films were being screened in Xiamen, Zhangzhou, and other places. The company immediately reported this to the local company bureaus, and the films were seized. It is now known that Lin and Xu are in Shanghai, residing at the Central Hotel on Wuma Road. Tianyi Company reported this to the constables, who arrested Lin and Xu and filed charges of embezzlement and fraud with the Special Court. A preliminary hearing was held the day before yesterday afternoon, with lawyers from both sides presenting their cases. Due to the lateness of the hour, the hearing was rescheduled. Accusation of Infringement of Freedom Qu Hanqing, through his lawyer, claimed in the criminal court of the French Concession court that the plaintiff previously partnered with Yang Shunqing and Yang Siqing in a contracting business, with the plaintiff providing the funds and receiving the payments. A contract was signed as evidence. Subsequently, they contracted to build a house for a certain family. However, the defendants collected the payments and used them privately, disregarding the plaintiff's funds and ignoring his inquiries. The defendants are therefore guilty of embezzlement, and he requests an investigation and the recovery of his funds, totaling over 9,000 taels of silver. The defendant, Yang Siqing, through his lawyer Zhang Cang, argued that although his client initially partnered with the plaintiff, he was not involved in the handling of money. The funds he handled were only used to pay for minor expenses. His client declared his withdrawal from the partnership with the plaintiff and Yang Shunqing in August of last year. However, last month, the plaintiff falsely claimed to invite his client to a tea house and secretly arranged for a detective to take him to the police station for detention. This constitutes an infringement of freedom, and he requests compensation for the losses. Yang Shunqing, also through his lawyer, denied the embezzlement. The judge ordered a further review. Young Woman Requests Separate Residence Pending Judgment The Parties Cannot Reconcile Wu Hu, a young woman from Yangzhou, previously engaged a lawyer to sue her husband, Wu Jiegen, in the criminal court of the French Concession court, accusing him of neglecting his duty to provide support and of abusive behavior, and requesting permission to live separately and to receive alimony of 50,000 yuan. Another hearing was held the day before yesterday. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that the previous instruction to attempt reconciliation had been unsuccessful, as the defendant showed no sincerity and never contacted the plaintiff for discussion. He therefore requested a judgment based on the plaintiff's request. The defendant's lawyer argued that the defendant had seven siblings and that the family property was managed by the eldest brother. The amount requested by the plaintiff was therefore difficult for the defendant to pay. The court noted that the parties could not reconcile and ordered a review pending judgment. Tianxiang Tobacco Company Sues to Recover Losses Tianxiang Tobacco Company, through its lawyer, filed a criminal complaint in the French Concession Court, stating that in April of this year, the plaintiff purchased five barrels of American tobacco leaves from Lu Ziqing, the manager of Jinlong Tobacco Leaf Company, for a price of 800 taels plus 205 yuan. However, the defendant, Lu Ziqing, filled the American tobacco leaf barrels with inferior Chinese goods and sold them to the plaintiff. The plaintiff did not notice this at the time of purchase and used the leaves to make cigarettes, which were then shipped to other ports for sale. Subsequently, the plaintiff received numerous letters of complaint from customers, which greatly impacted the plaintiff's business. The plaintiff used to use the best American tobacco leaves to manufacture cigarettes under the names of Aiman, Yuman, Hongxing, and Baojian, with an average monthly sales volume of over 300 cartons, each with a profit of 7 yuan, totaling 2,100 yuan. Since the use of the defendant's inferior goods, the plaintiff has suffered significant losses. The defendant is therefore guilty of the crime of breach of trust under Article 363 of the Criminal Law, and the plaintiff requests an investigation and the recovery of 100,000 yuan in damages. The defendant, Lu Ziqing, also through his lawyer, argued that Jinlong Tobacco Leaf Company is a US-owned company and that the transactions were conducted directly between the manager and the plaintiff. The defendant has no relationship with the matter and is merely a comprador who earns commissions and is not responsible for the quality of the goods. Judge Zhu ordered the defendant, Lu Ziqing, to provide a reliable guarantor for his release and to await the appointment of an accountant to investigate the actual losses suffered by the plaintiff before further hearing. Lost Boy Found The police officers of the Third District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau found a lost boy at the Lan Ni Du ferry in Pudong yesterday. The boy stated that his name is Du Amao, he is 13 years old, from Pudong, and he is an apprentice at the Zhou Zhengxing dowry shop on Beijing Road. He got lost while searching for his mother in Pudong. He was sent to the General Bureau for Lost and Found. Local News Two A Hurricane in This Port Yesterday A hurricane that had not visited for a long time suddenly appeared on the high seas outside the mouth of the Yangtze River yesterday. Due to its impact on this port, in addition to the heavy thunderstorms before dawn (around 2:00 or 3:00 yesterday morning), there was also a strong wind in the early morning, blowing fiercely eastward. In the afternoon, the wind became even stronger, with a howling sound that did not subside until dawn. The weather turned cold, and it was already chilly to wear a jacket. According to a report from the Yangjingbang Observatory yesterday afternoon, the center of the hurricane had reached the north of the mouth of the Yangtze River, and its trend was towards the northeast and east, continuing with low pressure. Strong Wind Breaks Flagpole Injures Constable and Passerby The Injuries Are Serious and Life-Threatening A flag was hanging on the roof of the Cloth Exchange on Aixi Road in the Public Concession. Due to the strong wind, the flagpole was broken by the wind around 3:00 yesterday afternoon and fell into the road, hitting Constable No. 2721 on the head and abdomen, and a passerby, He Baoge (43 years old), on the face and head. Zhao Congzhang Commits Suicide Due to Pessimism Unlimited Complaints in His Suicide Note It Must Be Due to Nervous Stimulation Zhao Congzhang, a student in the training class of the Ministry of Communications Telegraph School on Wangjia Pier Road in the South City of this port, suffered from nervous disorders and often felt pessimistic about life. On the 13th of this month, he once attempted to commit suicide by jumping into the Huangpu River, but was rescued by the guards at Guan Bridge and survived. However, on the morning of the 15th, he disappeared again. His colleagues at the school, fearing that the same thing would happen again, sent letters to the water and land police authorities to inquire and investigate his whereabouts. Last night, the school received a phone call from the Nanmatou Lifesaving Bureau, stating that Zhao's body had floated to the surface of the Huangpu River and had been recovered. They requested that someone come to identify the body. The school sent personnel to identify the body, which was confirmed to be Zhao. Thus, the mystery of Zhao Congzhang's disappearance was solved. The details of the student's suicide are recorded as follows: Family Situation Zhao was 25 years old, from Hepu County, Guangdong Province. He graduated from the county high school. His father had passed away early, but his mother was still alive. His elder brother, Congwen, is currently the director of the Bengbu Telegraph Bureau. The family is moderately well-off and can live comfortably. After graduating from high school, Zhao did not have a suitable career for a while. Therefore, he was introduced by his elder brother to practice reporting at the Telegraph Bureau for three years. Entering the Telegraph Industry In recent years, the transportation authorities, in order to rectify the telegraph administration, have formulated methods for identifying and examining telegraph students from various bureaus. Those who have not passed the examination will not be employed. Although Zhao had been working at the Telegraph Bureau for several years, he had not passed the examination and did not meet the requirements. This summer, the bureau reported him to the ministry, and after being identified and examined in the four regions of Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, and Sichuan, the ministry considered him to be promising. He was ordered to go to the Telegraph School for half a year of supplementary study before a decision was made on whether to retain him. Social Stimulation Over the years, Zhao served in the telegraph industry. In his spare time, he often discussed social, political, economic, and occupational issues with his colleagues. Seeing the darkness of society, the corruption of politics, the lack of occupational security, and the instability of life, he was greatly stimulated psychologically, and his nerves became weak. The idea of being pessimistic about life arose spontaneously. Since entering the school this summer, he has been influenced by new ideas, which has increased his sadness. He deeply felt that the great China was in a state of civil war all year round, the people were suffering, the country was in turmoil, and the telegraph industry was on the verge of bankruptcy. He thought it was useless to live and not worth regretting to die. On the morning of the 13th, he left a letter and left the school. Decided to Commit Suicide He wandered around Guan Bridge and Huangpu riverside. When the guards saw that he intended to commit suicide, they immediately rescued him and escorted him back to school. The school authorities and classmates persuaded him, but Zhao was determined to die. At 5:00 am on the 15th, he left his residence wearing a yellow sports shirt and pants and did not return all night. His colleagues became suspicious and sent letters to the water and land police authorities to pay attention to the search. Yesterday, the Lifesaving Bureau telegraphed that the second suicide had resulted in death. The bad news spread, and all the colleagues at the school deeply regretted it. The school telegraphed the student's family to send someone to Shanghai to handle the funeral arrangements. It is reported that they also plan to hold a memorial service. Contents of the Suicide Note Zhao was stimulated by society, which led him to commit suicide. The suicide note contained more than a thousand words, and the words were full of anger and leaped on the paper. Excerpts of the key points are as follows: "Today's world is declining, people's hearts are not ancient, the country is in turmoil, the people are suffering, the social system is full of miasma, private affairs are important, public affairs are light, politics are corrupt, the economy is bankrupt, the telegraph industry is becoming more dangerous, there is no occupational security, and life is unstable. My seven-foot body, Zhao Congzhang, is useless to live and not worth regretting to die. Instead of stealing life, it is better to die. I am dead, I am determined to die. Although my body is dead, my expectations for the improvement of society are even greater. I hope that the Chinese people will be alerted by my death, rise up and catch up, improve society, enrich people's livelihood, so that political clarity and national independence can be realized. There is great hope," and so on. Commercial News and Finance

Last Week’s Gold Market Still Favorable, Appropriate Value Swap Period, Major Players Strongly Raised Prices

Last week's gold market situation experienced slight changes, initially weak then firm. Coinciding with the swap period, the December market has opened, with bullish parties actively buying in, comparatively higher than last month. Prices were pushed up to 9 taels and some change, greatly stimulating the bearish side as they were pressured by major bullish players. Tracing back to the October period, reaching every three-month mark, premiums of over 30 taels have actually been posted. As for October market prices, they softened from firm at the start of the week, finally falling to 60 taels and 9 mace on October 14th (Tuesday). By Thursday (the swap day), it had risen to 73 and a half taels. Within these four days, the difference amounted to 12 taels and 6 mace. However, the closing price was 68 taels and 4 mace, an increase of 2 taels and 7 mace compared to last Saturday (October 11th).

The December market started trading from the 16th, but due to the swap-induced price increase, it was lower than November. The opening price was 63 taels and 8 mace. Later, due to sales by major players such as Yu Dafu, Xingyong, etc., it suddenly plummeted to 57 taels and 2 mace, entering a fluctuating pattern. However, generally, bearish parties were eager to buy back in, and by the weekend, it had already surged past the 70 tael mark. Nonetheless, there was also a 13 tael and 4 mace retracement within those three days. The final result was 70 taels and 6 mace, an increase of 6 taels and 8 mace compared to the first day's opening price.

However, there were no special news in the overseas silver market. Foreign silver bars increased by .0625 compared to the previous Saturday, with a total fluctuation of only .1875. The American silver market was balanced, with a fluctuation of .375. Exchange rates for sterling were level, and Japanese exchange rates decreased by only .25, contrasting with the gold market and almost becoming a divergence.

In summary, gold prices were forcibly raised by major players during the swap period. According to investigations, among the firms, bullish parties such as the Dalian group held approximately over 1,000 contracts, Fuchang, Yuanheng approximately 10,000 contracts, Yufeng Yong six to seven thousand contracts, Chengfeng Yong three to four thousand contracts. Bearish parties included Dadecheng with approximately 6,000 contracts, Yuanxing, Yongtai, Kangrun, Taixing, Hongxing, etc., also belonged to the bearish side, while Hengxing Shengda was rumored to have switched from bullish to bearish. The total amount of swap contracts for this period was 46,000 to 47,000, with over 10,000 contracts yet to be settled. As for the gold collateral, according to the daily gold quotation, it was initially pressed around 50 taels, but by the weekend, it was only pressed at over 40 taels. The existing bare gold bar market had limited inventory. Term collateral was approximately 18 to 19 taels higher. The following is a record of the situation throughout the week.

The Market Shape Shifts from Weak to Strong with Slight Ups and Downs

Starting on Monday, October 13th, the initial opening price for the November gold collateral increased by 2 taels and 8 mace, to 68 and a half taels. Due to the large contract decrease, confidence improved. Afterwards, major players divested, with Hengxing, Shengda, Yuansheng, etc. leaning towards selling, and almost a 6 tael drop in the afternoon. The exchange market also seemed to loosen, so the resulting price was 1 tael and 8 mace lower than the previous Saturday. The next day, large contracts increased by 0.125, silver prices were inactive, and exchange rates increased by half a grade. Internal conditions were also weak, so the gold market fell to 60 taels and 9 mace in the morning session, then turned slightly peaceful, with the afternoon session closing at 64 taels. On this day, the fluctuation was only 3 taels and 6 mace.

On Wednesday, large contracts slightly increased, exchange rates were stable, and with the swap period approaching, bearish parties bought in, causing the demand to exceed supply in the market, pushing prices to 70 taels in the afternoon. In particular, fellow firms had already pre-arranged swaps, initially with bullish parties offering a premium of 6 taels, then 6 and a half to 5 and a half taels, and later transactions at 6 taels, raising the market price. The closing price was 69 taels and 6 mace, an increase of 5 taels and 6 mace compared to the previous day, with a difference of 5 taels and 9 mace between the morning and afternoon sessions.

The following day, the silver market was slightly lower, and internal exchange rates showed firmness. However, banks' willingness to sell remained unabated. The gold market coincided with the swap period, initially with bearish parties offering a premium of 7 taels, then gradually raising it, reaching over 9 taels, and even nearing 10 taels. The result was 9 taels, which was raised by powerful major players. The general bearish parties were in a pessimistic state. Compelled by the environment, they had no choice but to suffer a painful blow. The November market had no more transactions. The initial December contract was 63 taels and 8 mace, followed by 4 taels. Then, due to Yu Dafu, Xingyong, Hengxing, Dadecheng, etc., leaning towards selling, it suddenly dropped to 57 taels and 2 mace, breaking the 60 tael mark. However, in the afternoon session, Yuancheng, Jinan, Daixinheng covered short positions, and Taixing, etc., followed suit, resulting in a surge of 6 to 7 taels, reaching 65 taels and 8 mace, with a slight one or two tael fluctuation afterwards, closing at 4 mace and 8 mace, with a total retracement of 8 taels and 6 mace in one day.

The next day, large contracts did not change, and silver prices increased, so the initial collateral market was weak. With no movement in the United States, the silver market was mediocre, opening at 62 taels. Later, major players sold, retreating to 58 taels and 8 mace. Then, major players stepped out, rising by 3 taels. In the afternoon, Hengxing, Taixing, Dadecheng, etc., divested, once dropping by 3 taels, reaching 60 taels and 4 mace, immediately rebounding by 1 tael. However, it was still 3 taels and 1 mace lower than the previous day. The market situation was exceptionally uncertain, seemingly in a fluctuating state.

On Saturday, although large contracts increased, silver prices did not change, and private telegrams were lower. With indecision in Japan and the United States, the gold market did not weaken. Afterwards, Yu Da covered short positions for clients, and Zhifeng, Yongfeng, Taikangrun, etc., also followed suit. With sterling reducing by half a grade and internal conditions also tight, there was a strong desire for change, suddenly surging through the 70 tael mark, resulting in 70 taels and 6 mace, and then rising beyond 70 taels. Major bullish players had considerable pulling power, but no one dared to go short, fearing suppression. Therefore, it was 8 taels and 9 mace higher than the previous day, with a large difference of 10 taels in half a day.

In general, the volume of listed contracts was limited, and bullish parties were quite optimistic. The following is a table of high and low prices for the British, American, and Indian silver markets and exchange rates.

Overseas Silver Markets Unanimously Retract

Yesterday, London news reported that large silver bars retracted again. Funds from China sold out, and funds from India and China again bought in at low prices. Market conditions were calm after the market closed. Near and far term silver both retracted by 0.125, both at 16 pence 625 (equivalent to 1 shilling 7 pence 6875 in British gold). A New York report stated that American silver also retracted by 0.25, with the current spot price at 0.35875. The exchange rate of British to American currency plus 0.03125, and the exchange rate of American to British remained unchanged at $4.86. The exchange rate of Japanese to American currency remained unchanged at $49.625. The exchange rate of British to Japanese currency remained at 1 shilling and 0.03217. The Shanghai sterling rate decreased by 0.125, calculated as 1 shilling and 7 pence 625. The Bombay spot price decreased by 0.5 anna, calculated as 47 rupees and 0.08 anna.

Money Market Tightens Suddenly This Week

Yesterday the bank was closed, resulting in a sudden tightening of money. The morning interbank rate opened at 0.02, and the afternoon rate was also 0.017. The morning foreign interest rate was 0.0726375, and the afternoon rate was 0.072625. The transaction volume for the morning foreign exchange drawing was 445,000, and the afternoon volume was 193,000. The banknote volume was only 40,000 in the afternoon. The over-the-counter banknote volume was 65,000 in the morning and 30,000 in the afternoon. Money shops collected over 33 million in silver and over 2.7 million in foreign currency. Remittances from various routes were over 300,000. Transactions among smaller firms were over 400,000.

The morning price of small Jiangnan foreign coins was 0.0644, and the afternoon price was the same. The transaction volume was 5,000 jiao in the morning and 1,000 jiao in the afternoon. The morning price of small Guangdong foreign coins was 0.0637125, and the afternoon price was 0.0637. The transaction volume was 140,000 jiao in the morning and 75,000 jiao in the afternoon. Copper coins were at 390.500 per thousand, slightly lower than the previous day by 500.

Last Week's Bond Prices Fluctuated and Trended Weaker

1929 Customs Duty Bonds Fell by 5 Yuan, Demobilization Bonds Fell by a Little Over 1 Yuan

Other bonds remained stable, with a total transaction volume of 40.02 million yuan.

The trading volume of various government bonds in the securities market was low last week, with a total volume of only 67,4800 yuan. Other bonds had transaction volumes of only a few thousand yuan each. The futures market was also as calm as before. The number of buyers and sellers in the market each day was even lower than before, as the overall environment was gloomy and major players were adopting a wait-and-see approach, resulting in very few transactions. Investigations revealed that the transaction volume was over 8.7 million yuan for the first two days of the week, 5.7 million yuan on Wednesday, and only over 4 million yuan on Friday, the quietest day. Saturday was slightly better, with a transaction volume of over 7.1 million yuan. The total transaction volume for the week was 40.02 million yuan, approximately 2 million yuan less than the previous week. Demobilization Bonds remained relatively active, while Reorganization and Customs Duty Bonds were very calm. The trading of 1919 Customs Duty Bonds was relatively lively, and 96 Bonds were also not inactive. However, other bonds remained scarce.

Regarding the fluctuations of various bonds last week, with the exception of 1919 Customs Duty Bonds, other government bonds remained very stagnant, with daily fluctuations of only a few jiao, without any significant declines. The bond market environment was calm, and the financial situation was stable, so major buyers and sellers were adopting a wait-and-see approach, resulting in a very balanced supply and demand. The bond prices were therefore in a state of neither rising nor falling. However, 1919 Customs Duty Bonds were actively sold by major players on Monday, with a sharp decline of over 3 yuan. On Tuesday, they declined by approximately 1 yuan, and although they rose by approximately 0.49 jiao later, they still declined by approximately 1 yuan by the end of the week. Because 1919 Customs Duty Bonds were recently issued, although there were active sellers in the market, investors had not yet paid close attention to them.

As a result, compared to the previous week, 1919 Customs Duty Bond futures fell by 5 yuan, spot prices fell by 3.5 yuan, Demobilization Bond spot prices fell by a little over 2.3 yuan, and futures also fell by a little over 1 yuan. Other bonds also weakened slightly, with declines of approximately 0.5 yuan. Food and Grains

Rice Market Decline Slightly Stabilizes

Zhabei: Yesterday, over thirty rice boats arrived at inner wharves, and sales activity turned slightly active. High-quality new japonica rice saw a decrease of two jiao, opening at 15.3 yuan. Medium and lower grades generally experienced no fluctuations, as high-quality japonica rice had increased significantly recently, while medium and lower grades had seen larger price reductions. Therefore, the market stabilized, and the situation immediately changed. Although the japonica market has now stabilized, it is still not easy to gain a firm foothold. The arrival and sales of thin rice were balanced, and prices remained unchanged. Indica rice and wharf-picked rice gradually became consistent, with very low sales volumes and inactive customer routes. The arrival of foreign rice impeded progress, making the market quite sluggish.

Large Market: After the revision of the jiao, the Dujian market has stabilized, with brisk retail sales and a slightly stable market. High-quality goods were at 11.9 yuan. After the previous sharp decline in guest indica rice, shipments from the producing areas to Shanghai were scarce, so there was no sign of excessive price reductions. In fact, rice around 9.5 yuan meets the demands of the civilian market. Although old white rice has stabilized, due to the presence of new rice, buying interest is extremely sluggish. Therefore, prices have not softened, but the market has already weakened. Yin yuan opened at 14 jiao. The rice market throughout the day had a fluctuating trend.

Shanghai South: Yesterday, sources arrived continuously downstream, but sales were sluggish. New Changbang japonica rice continued to trend downward, opening at around 15 yuan. Some inquiries were made about Sutong white japonica rice from Chongming and Tongzhou, but these were only scattered transactions, and prices softened by about two jiao. Top-quality goods are approaching the 14 yuan mark. The situation for thin rice and white rice from Nanbang Jiaoli Qingpu Chonggu Sijing, etc., was quite calm. In past years, japonica and thin rice prices have generally been comparable, but this time there is a large disparity, so people generally hope that thin rice may stabilize. Indica and Dujian rice continue to soften, due to a lack of inquiries and sluggish buying interest. High-quality goods can still be maintained, while lower grades saw small price reductions of about a jiao. The state of the japonica and indica rice markets here has stabilized. In general, the arrival and sales of Yin yuan were sluggish, and the overall market slightly recovered by one jiao, with high Yin yuan opening at 14 yuan.

Sugar Market: Minghua Factory's Shipments Expected Soon, Japanese Sugar Prices Likely to Decline

Yesterday, the sugar market received telegrams from the producing areas. As it was Sunday, no telegrams arrived. At the market, quotations were flat, and transactions were very low. Shipments of No. 24 Dutch coarse granulated white sugar were quite plentiful, with asking prices at 7 taels 8 mace and a half, and slightly higher prices at 7 taels 9 mace. Inquiries were quiet, and some buyers had slight interest, but their bidding prices were low, so no transactions occurred. The market for medium granulated white sugar was very abundant, and the trend was weaker, with a general sense of abundant supply and no demand. No. 8 Dutch red sugar was at 6 taels 3 mace. Although activity was sluggish, the market remained strong. N mark Japanese sugar was at 7 taels 8 mace, and YT mark was at 7 taels 7 mace, with demand also quiet. YP mark was at 8 taels, with prices firm due to shortages. J mark was at 8 taels 1 mace and a half, an increase of 5 fen from the previous time, and the market was brisk. However, Minghua Factory is scheduled to start production today, and shipments are expected soon. At a time when sales are sluggish, the future trend has a pessimistic outlook.

North-South Goods: New Red and Black Dates Arriving Gradually

The first batch of genuine new Tianjin red dates only arrived in twenty or so packages. As the first buyers had sold them at 14 taels to establish a base price, the second batch of over a thousand packages arrived the day before yesterday via Xin Feng and Shun Tian ships. It was reported yesterday that they had already been released, with the best top-quality dates opening at 12 taels 6 mace. The next two to three grades were priced at 9 taels 6 mace to 7 taels 6 mace, and the subsequent ones at 12 taels 4 mace to 11 taels 4 mace, with the two to three grades priced at 8 taels to 6 taels. If more arrive in the future, there is hope for price declines.

The day before yesterday, the Guangzhou and Xinjiang ships Guang Sheng and Xinjiang each brought approximately 3,000 packages of new black dates, mostly in the upper and middle grades. However, at present, sales in various merchant groups are most active for the lower grades. For example, the Fujian groups of Xinghua and Quanzhou recently sold 500 to 600 packages, and the sales volume of the Wenzhou and Taizhou groups was also considerable. Therefore, market prices have increased by 5 to 6 qian compared to before.

Silk and Tea

Silk Market: Silk Market Gradually Showing Vitality

Jiangzhe Silk Factories Suspend Operations, Silk Production Decreases Daily, European Sales Begin

Chinese Merchants Maintain High Prices, Factory Prices Tend to Increase Sharply

Last week, the silk market in Shanghai saw a gradual turnaround. As silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces successively announced the suspension of operations, silk production decreased daily, and hoarders began to accumulate stocks. Overseas silk weaving factories also showed a tendency to purchase both futures and spot silk. In the first half of the week, European and American telegrams were still slow to reach Shanghai. Only a few firms took the opportunity to make progress. However, manufacturers, facing scarce raw materials and high costs for their existing silk stocks, are currently petitioning the government for relief funds, adopting a passive attitude and insisting on high prices before selling, resulting in increasingly few transactions.

By the second half of the week, European sales of Yokohama Japanese silk had begun, and silk prices gradually increased by ten to twenty yen per day. By the weekend, European and American telegrams to Shanghai factories became more frequent and smooth, and various firms began to seek supplies, causing the market to suddenly become active. Factory prices have the potential to increase sharply. Unfortunately, silk supplies remain insufficient, and most of the silk stocks held by factories are in the hands of financial institutions, making it difficult to expect a rapid increase in transactions.

The total transaction volume for the week was approximately 200 packages of silk futures and spot goods. The actual volume of raw silk shipped out was over 700 packages. The prices of overseas Chinese silk generally followed the trend of rising Yokohama Japanese silk, but were still relatively flat and weak in the first half of the week.

Yesterday Morning Bandits Murdered on Beijing-Shanghai Train 102

Train Staff Member Died in the Line of Duty

The Culprit Has Been Captured

At approximately 1:40 AM yesterday morning, the 28th night express train from Beijing to Shanghai on the Beijing-Shanghai line, while approaching the Zhenjiang mountain cave, was moving extremely slowly due to the uphill gradient. Suddenly, a person dressed in military uniform and wielding a handgun, resembling a bandit, jumped onto the train guard's carriage. The train guard, Chang Rongli, and the accompanying luggage clerk, Zhu Chungan, realizing this was no good person, and given the carriage's status as an official vehicle and its limited space, repeatedly and politely asked him to get off the train, but he ignored them. The train guard and others, seeing him unreasonable, declared they would notify the military police on the front train to come and remove him. Unexpectedly, this statement offended him. In desperation, he immediately drew his handgun and fired five shots at the staff. The luggage clerk was the most severely wounded, struck by a bullet that entered his left cheek and exited his right neck, causing an immediate and profuse flow of blood, rendering him unconscious. The train guard sustained a graze wound to his left shoulder, which was not serious. After the incident, the bandit jumped off the train between Danyang and Xinfeng stations and fled. However, passengers and other government personnel, as well as the escorting military police, did not hear anything due to the train being in motion and the loud noise. It was not until the train reached Danyang station that the incident was discovered. A telegram was immediately sent to the Seventh Company of the Second Battalion of the First Regiment of the National Government Guard Brigade stationed at Xinfeng station, requesting troops to search and arrest the perpetrator. Simultaneously, a telegram was urgently sent to Changzhou station, requesting the preparation of a medical car to transport the severely injured luggage clerk to Wujin Hospital for treatment overnight. Unfortunately, due to the critical nature of the wound, excessive blood loss, and the jolting of the train, he could not be saved and died at the hospital at 6:00 AM yesterday morning. It was also learned that the perpetrator had been captured by the stationed troops near Yangqi outside Xinfeng station at approximately 7:00 AM yesterday morning and is currently under interrogation. The train guard, having sustained minor injuries, continued with the train to Shanghai to report the facts of the incident. However, as yesterday was a Sunday, all departments were on holiday, so the Railway Bureau has not yet determined how to handle the case or the compensation for the deceased staff member.

Difficulties for Chinese Citizens Going Abroad 103

Dutch Government Increases Head Tax on Overseas Chinese

Overseas Chinese Associations Request Serious Government Negotiations

There are over 1.8 million Chinese people residing in the Dutch East Indies. In the late Qing Dynasty, Chinese people could reach those lands with just a few tens of dollars due to competition among commercial ships, which made fares extremely low. Passport fees and other expenses were also minimal. Consequently, many poor and hardworking people from the southeastern coast went to the Dutch East Indies to make a living. In the early years of the Republic of China, the Dutch government, in order to limit the entry of Chinese, imposed a head tax of 25 guilders (each guilder equivalent to 1.5 Chinese dollars) on each Chinese immigrant upon landing, calling it a "dock tax." In 1919, it added another 25 guilders, and in 1923, another 50 guilders. In total, each person going to the Dutch East Indies had to pay a dock tax of 100 guilders, plus over a hundred dollars for ship fare and passport, requiring a self-provided 400 Chinese dollars to leave the country. In April of this year, the Dutch Colonial Council resolved to further increase the head tax on overseas Chinese by 50 guilders. At the time, Lin Youren, a member of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission of the National Government, petitioned the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to order the Consul-General in Java to negotiate strictly with the Dutch government. As a result, the Dutch government agreed to postpone the matter. However, in June, the Dutch Colonial Council reintroduced the old proposal and resolved that, starting from January 1, 1931, immigrants from the Far East would have to pay an additional 50 guilders in dock tax per person. Since approximately 200,000 Chinese people travel to the Dutch East Indies each year, each paying a dock tax of 150 guilders (equivalent to 225 Chinese dollars), the Dutch government could collect a total of 45 million Chinese dollars in dock taxes annually, a staggering sum. With Chinese people burdened by such significant taxes, they will be hesitant to proceed, and the poor in the country will have no opportunity to go abroad to make a living. The Shanghai General Association of Overseas Chinese Federations has petitioned the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate seriously with the Dutch government, urging them to revoke the resolution to increase the dock tax. The association recently received telegram number 282 from the Ministry, stating: "To the Overseas Chinese Federation, we have received your telegram. The Consul-General in Java replied via telegram, stating that it is not limited to immigrants from the Far East; all countries in Europe and America are treated equally. The Ministry, considering the significant impact on overseas Chinese, has instructed the embassy in Japan and the Consul-General in Java to continue negotiations separately, and has also informed the Chinese embassy in Japan, requesting them to ask the Japanese government to fundamentally revoke the original proposal. We are replying." The Overseas Chinese Association believes that although the Dutch government's increase in head tax on overseas Chinese applies equally to all countries in Europe and America, there are over 1.8 million Chinese residing in the Dutch East Indies, while only about 4,000 Japanese reside there, and only a few hundred people from the United Kingdom and the United States. Therefore, it held a special meeting yesterday (the 19th) morning and decided to submit another petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting the implementation of revolutionary diplomacy, and sending telegrams to the ambassadors and consuls in The Hague and Java, urging them to quickly unite with the ambassadors and consuls of other countries to protest the Dutch Colonial Council's resolution to increase the immigration tax for immigrants from the Far East to 150 guilders per person, in order to achieve the fundamental goal of cancellation. Because the number of our people residing there is higher than in any other country, our ambassadors and consuls should take the lead and unite with the ambassadors and consuls of other countries to protest together.

Rice Industry Workers' Union Advises Shop Owners to Refuse to Sell Japanese Rice 104

Important Notice from the Council of the Shanghai Rice and Grain Industry Workers' Union (Posted in Shops on October 19)

Notice Regarding the Serious Matter of Resisting the Sale of Japanese Rice in Shops: After investigating the case of opposing Japan's self-serving and harmful economic invasion policy, which involves hoarding large quantities of rice in warehouses and transporting it to China for sale, plundering the interests of our country's farmers, industrialists, and merchants, Sun Zhentong has advised rice merchants and requested authorities to resist, as reported in various newspapers in recent days. Furthermore, according to the instructions of the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau, Chinese people are not allowed to purchase Japanese rice. Rice merchant leaders, the Guild, the Jiagu Association, and the Rice Milling Association have successively expressed their strict opposition, issuing notices that no one is allowed to mill or sell Japanese rice. We believe that this matter concerns the livelihood of the people and is a foreign disaster. Our union members, serving in the industry, cannot shirk our responsibility. Our patriotic hearts will not fall behind others. We should exercise our freedom of speech and reasonably advise shop owners, managers, and those in charge to unanimously resist and never sell Japanese rice. If anyone is unpersuaded, found to be selling Japanese rice, or violating the ban, we urge you to investigate and report them secretly so that we can expose and punish the traitors. Those who conceal information will be equally liable. This notice is specifically to inform members to strictly prevent, supervise, and advise, and not to feign compliance, lest they commit a crime. This notice is to be shown to all comrades in your establishment.

Zhejiang Silk Cocoon Merchants Request Refusal to Purchase Japanese Cocoons 105

Letter to the Silk Factory Trade Association

The case of Japanese cocoons entering the country has attracted the attention of all sectors of the country. Zhejiang Province cocoon merchants, specifically for this matter, organized the All-Zhejiang Cocoon Industry Association Federation to discuss countermeasures, which held its first meeting in Shanghai on the previous Sunday. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday, the association, using the name of Zhejiang silk factories, sent a letter to the Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association, asking it to forward the message to all silk factories in Shanghai to not purchase Japanese cocoons for silk reeling in order to save Chinese cocoons. The original letter is recorded below: "Dear Sirs, the purchasing and transporting of Japanese cocoons by the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Silk Cocoon General Association is an invasion of our country's silk cocoon sales and is extremely harmful. Letters and telegrams have been sent, calling and running around, even though our tongues have been parched, and those who speak are earnestly trying to persuade while those who listen are indifferent. We have neither the ability to urge the government to awaken and stop this, nor the financial resources to maintain the suspension of the cocoon industry. The only plan for now is to ask our silk factory colleagues to not purchase Japanese cocoons for silk reeling. There are two reasons for this: (1) We Chinese people should support Chinese goods and purchase Chinese cocoons, in order to show a little patriotism. (2) The sales of Chinese silk have not been extensive recently and it is difficult to compete. The quality of the work is not good, which cannot be denied, but the reason why it can still be exported and occupy a portion of the market is thanks to its natural beauty (tough quality and smooth color). Now, if Japanese cocoons are mixed in, on the one hand, its beauty will be lost, and on the other hand, the work will not be as good as the Japanese. Once it cannot be trusted or exported, it will be too late to regret. Silk merchants and cocoon merchants will perish together, and China's sericulture industry will also be in a desperate situation. A small spark can start a prairie fire. The urgency of the situation requires immediate action. This association proposes the above, and hopes that you will carefully consider it."

Chu Minyi Will Return to China from the United States 106

Chu Minyi and his staff, who went to Belgium to participate in the Exposition, are preparing to return to China. According to a fast letter sent from Liege, France, on the 2nd of this month, Chu is scheduled to cross the Atlantic from France to the United States on the 20th of this month, and then return to China from the United States, expecting to arrive in Shanghai on December 14th. As for other personnel participating in the Exposition, such as Mr. Tian Shouchang, they are currently packing and generally plan to return to China by land, and are expected to arrive in Shanghai by the end of November.

Merrell Sails for Hong Kong Today 107

Consulting with the Hong Kong Government

On Matters Such as Anti-Smuggling and Taxation

Mr. Merrell, the Inspector General of Customs, traveled to Hong Kong last winter to consult with the Hong Kong government authorities on the establishment of tax collection and anti-smuggling agencies in Hong Kong, and has obtained substantial understanding. However, the terms were not consistent. There was a proposal for a second trip to Hong Kong this spring, but unexpectedly, the Central Plains War broke out after the travel dates were set. Merrell was unable to leave Shanghai due to heavy responsibilities. Now that the war has ended and the situation has been renewed, the matter cannot be delayed. Therefore, it was decided that he would depart from Shanghai for Hong Kong this Monday to negotiate in person. Since the implementation of our country's new tariff, foreign goods have been taxed heavily, and merchants are engaging in more smuggling than before in order to avoid heavy taxation. Moreover, Hong Kong and Guangdong are close at hand, and prevention should be approached from both sides, otherwise it will be difficult to achieve results. The Hong Kong authorities already understand this point, but the British side seems to have made excessive demands on the terms, so the matter was interrupted. Now that our country's domestic turmoil has been quelled, the central government is consolidated, and its international status has increased accordingly. All diplomacy is easier to handle than before, so Merrell's trip south this time is very optimistic.

The Information Division of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Discussion Group Will Move 110

Moving into the Foreign Affairs Office on the 25th

The Shanghai branch of the Information Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Foreign Affairs Discussion Group, originally located at No. 1066 Shanzhong Road, will move into the remaining buildings of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at Fenglin Bridge on the 25th due to the expiration of the lease. The Discussion Group will be located at the original site of the former Foreign Affairs Department's Receiving and Dispatching Office, and the Information Division will be located at the remaining buildings of the Foreign Affairs Building. The Ministry's radio station will be relocated to another rented building due to radio wave interference with the Ministry of Communications' radio station.

The Dispute Over Factory Silk Inspection Will Be Resolved 111

Mediation by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

Since the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau implemented the public weight inspection of export factory silk on a trial basis six months ago, silk factories in Shanghai and Wuxi have suffered considerable losses and have appealed for its cancellation. The bureau has refused, leading to a strike by silk factories to protest. It is learned that the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau has stated that the public weight inspection of export silk is being carried out under the orders of the ministry and that the bureau has no authority to abolish it. It has reported the situation to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for instructions. The manufacturers have also petitioned the ministry to cancel the inspection to comply with public opinion. While both sides are awaiting instructions from the ministry, the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously invited both sides to a meeting to mediate. Zou Bingwen, director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, Miao Zhongxiu, director of the silk inspection department, Shen Huachen, chairman of the Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association, Zhu Jingan, standing committee member, and Huang Jinzhen, chairman of the Silk Cocoon General Association, were all in attendance. As a result of the mediation by the chairman (of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce) Wang Xiaolai, it was decided to devise a better solution so that silk merchants would no longer suffer unexpected losses. It is expected that this matter can be resolved peacefully.

Silk Factories to Convene Third Delegates' Conference 112

Delegates Will Petition in Beijing

Silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are suffering losses and suspending operations, and have resolved to appeal to the government to issue 10 million yuan in public bonds for the silk industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai to save the industry. They have sent delegates to Shanghai to form a special committee to handle this case. Two delegates' conferences have already been convened, and the outlines for the issuance of public bonds and the apportionment of debt have been agreed upon. A petition is currently being drafted, and it has been decided that after the third delegates' conference is convened on the 22nd of this month (this Wednesday), all fifteen delegates will take the petition to Beijing and present it to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, respectively, requesting approval and implementation to save the dying silk industry and the livelihoods of over 100,000 workers.

Cotton Exhibition Sampling Office Requests Transportation Prices 113

Letter to Transportation Companies

The Shanghai Sampling Office for the Cotton Exhibition of the National Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce sent letters to various transportation companies requesting prices for transporting the samples. The letter stated: The National Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is scheduled to open a cotton exhibition in Beijing on November 1st of this year and has established a Shanghai Sampling Office. All the exhibits and goods for sale will be gathered here and then transported to Beijing. According to the ministry's regulations, such exhibition goods are exempt from taxes with a passport from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Railways, and only half of the shipping fee is charged. We are now listing the conditions and hope that you will calculate the shipping fee per dan and provide a detailed reply. The conditions are: (1) The goods are purely cotton products. (2) The shipping location is from the factory to the train station. (3) The receiving location is the National Products Exhibition Hall at Huaiqing Bridge in Nanjing. (4) Taxes are completely exempt, with a passport from the ministry. (5) The railway freight rate is half price, with a passport from the ministry.

National Goods Association Sends Representatives to Suzhou 114

To Negotiate Matters Regarding the Exhibition in Suzhou

The China National Goods Maintenance Association and the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association have accepted the resolution of the Shanghai National Goods Trade Delegation and Factory Representatives Conference to hold a national goods mobile exhibition in Suzhou. First, the two associations will send staff to negotiate, and then a delegates' conference will be convened to form a preparatory committee. It is learned that the executive committees of the two associations held a joint meeting the day before yesterday afternoon and publicly elected Wang Jiean, Shen Shuyu, and Chen Yiting as representatives to go to Suzhou and negotiate with the Suzhou General Chamber of Commerce, the Youth Association, and other public organizations on Suzhou-Shanghai cooperation, the venue, the dates, accommodation, tax exemption, transportation, the opening date, and all other matters. It is reported that the three representatives departed on the night train last night.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Abolition of Tobacco Leaf Brokerage 115

The original plan to maintain that provinces and cities should not arbitrarily levy taxes should be upheld

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "On the 17th of this month, according to a letter from the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Industry Association, 'Our member, Huacheng Tobacco Company, reported in a letter from our assistant, Shen Xingde, from Tanfangzi, Qingzhou, that after arriving there to purchase tobacco leaves, Tanfang and Yangjiazhuang are both under the jurisdiction of Yidu County. Now, a broker named Zhang Zhiquan has fabricated a reason and presented it to the Yidu County government, announcing the collection of a 2% brokerage fee on buying and selling, which is actually a burden on merchants and the people. Moreover, after investigating the many areas along the route that produce tobacco leaves, why is Yidu County the only one that is different? All merchants believe that it is illegal. British and American tobacco merchants have gone to Qingdao to negotiate and have stopped bidding, and all our Chinese merchants are also stopping bidding and handling the matter in the same way, pending resolution. The county's announcement is enclosed for your information, and we request that you promptly report to the association, which will relay the situation to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and then telegraph the government and the Ministry of Finance to negotiate seriously and order the Shandong province to issue an order to the county to immediately cancel the brokerage fee so that merchants can transport their goods smoothly,' We at the company further verified that the tax burden on tobacco merchants is already very heavy, so how can they bear further extortion and exploitation? Therefore, this special letter, along with a copy of Yidu's announcement, is sent to your association for investigation. We earnestly request that you promptly forward it to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to relay it to the central government and the Ministry of Finance, requesting that they approve the telegraph order to the province to cancel this brokerage fee to maintain commerce and facilitate transportation. We hope that you will implement this quickly and provide us with a reply.'" A copy of the announcement from the Yidu County government was enclosed. After investigation, the goods within the scope of national tax collection should not be subject to any donations or taxes without the approval of the ministry, which has been ordered by the Executive Yuan to be strictly followed by the financial authorities of all provinces and cities. Tobacco tax is one of the national taxes, and local agencies absolutely cannot impose additional donations, which is beyond doubt. Now, Tanfangzi, which belongs to Yidu County in Shandong, actually has tobacco leaf brokerage agents similar to contractors who, under the pretext of being recognized for paying taxes, have requested the collection of a 2% brokerage fee on the buying and selling of tobacco leaves. The Yidu County government has even publicly announced its approval, disregarding the ministry's orders, arbitrarily increasing the burden on tobacco merchants, making it impossible to promote national tobacco leaves to the fullest extent, destroying the tax system, and increasing the burden on merchants. This is the worst of all. Therefore, we enclose a copy of the Yidu County announcement and request that your department verify and quickly issue a telegraph order to cancel the brokerage fee on tobacco leaves to relieve the people's difficulties by means of government orders.

Please Exempt Taiping Tea from Miscellaneous Taxes 116

National Goods Association Submits a Letter to the Ministry of Finance

Sun Fuxian, a tea merchant from Taiping, Anhui, residing in Shanghai, stated that when Taiping tea is transported to Beijing, in addition to paying regular taxes, it must also pay 22 miscellaneous taxes at various checkpoints, including the Xiahekou inspection fee, wharf registration fee, handling fee, permit fee, cancellation fee, likin, stamp fee, Xihua Customs skin tax, private fee, Nanling branch card cancellation fee, stamp fee, Wanzhi likin, Wuhu South Customs, Xiliangshan, Anhui Customs tail fee, Jiangsu Daxing Customs cancellation fee, stamp fee, Nanjing Xinhekou, Hanxing Customs, Shiyinqiao, and Shuiximen landing fee, totaling 9.49 yuan per permit. The excessive costs make it difficult to promote sales and is not conducive to revitalizing Chinese tea. He specifically requested the China National Goods Maintenance Association for assistance. It is learned that the association's executive committee has decided to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance to abolish the contractor system and implement a "one item, one tax" system, and to order the Anhui Provincial Tax Bureau to strictly prohibit miscellaneous taxes in order to facilitate sales and alleviate the difficulties of merchants.

There Will Be Unprecedentedly Fast Liners on the Sino-European Route 117

British Merchants Specially Build the Fastest Five Mail Ships

Japanese Shipping Companies Discuss Countermeasures

Since the Japanese Post Office added two new mail ships, Jingguomaru and Zhaoguomaru, to the Sino-European route, the British company "Great Britain" has been the leader in the Far East-Europe shipping industry. They are very reliable with ship schedules and have a high value on passenger service. Every fourteen days there is a boat to London, and they are well known for exporting silk and tea from Shanghai. They are still ranked number one in exporting lake silk and Chinese tea to Europe this year, even surpassing the Blue Funnel Line. Since adding five R-class ships with a net tonnage of 16,000 tons last year, the sea route from Shanghai to the United Kingdom has been reduced from forty-two days to thirty-eight days. In recent years, commercial shipping has trended towards fast ships, and exports of silk and tea have paid great attention to market conditions. Faster shipping means more freight. In order to maintain its special position as the number one company in the Far East, the British shipping company proposed building unprecedentedly fast ships to join the Sino-European route. Furthermore, the Blue Funnel Line is also building eight new-style express ships of 10,000 tons each, powered by motor engines, on the Shanghai-London route, with five of them already completed and soon to be in service. The Italian shipping company is also replacing four express ships to operate in China. The company has decided to build five more giant ships, each with 25,000 tons, with a maximum speed of 28 knots per hour and a normal speed of 23 knots per hour, compared to the current 18 knots per hour of various companies. The sea route between China and Britain can be reduced by five days. This is already under construction. These fast ships are unprecedented in the Far East-Europe route, operating exclusively on the Shanghai-London route, with the eastbound route also going to Yokohama, Japan. When the Japanese Post Office and Osaka Company received this news, they feared that the eighteen ships of the Japanese company currently operating on the European route would be overwhelmed after the strong-speed ships were put into service. In order to save the Sino-European Japanese shipping industry, they invited all Japanese shipping companies to discuss countermeasures to resist this. Fierce competition will occur between British and Japanese shipping companies on the Sino-European route.
